Fierce Battle Between Deng Tiemei's Troops and Japanese Army

Deng's Officers Arrive in Beiping to Discuss Situation at the Front

Dong Rongjiu's Troops Temporarily Withdraw to Original Defense Due to Lack of Ammunition

Special Dispatch from Beiping: The 28th Route of the National Salvation Army, led by Deng Tiemei, previously captured 15 Japanese instructors and translators in Xiuyan and executed them all. Upon hearing the news, the Japanese side sent troops to attack Deng's troops. Fierce battles took place several times in Huangtukan. An officer of Deng's troops arrived in Beiping yesterday (3rd) and discussed the battle situation in detail. He stated that our army previously captured nine Japanese instructors in Xiuyan. Later, the Japanese side sent four more Japanese and two translators from Shenyang to contact our army to rescue the captured Japanese. After our investigation, we found that their actions were secretive and were actually spying on our army's secrets. They were immediately detained, and on the 13th of last month, the Japanese and translators, 15 people in total, were executed. Upon receiving this news, the Japanese side sent more than 200 troops and colluded with Li Shoushan's Second Brigade of the Puppet Border Pacification Army to attack our army in three routes. Our side prepared defenses in advance and responded separately. The enemy's southern route arrived at Huangtukan in the southern third district of Fengcheng on the 17th of last month and encountered Zhu's regiment of our army in a fierce battle that lasted all day without a clear victor. Zhu's regiment retreated to Huangtukan, more than ten miles north, for strategic reasons. The enemy occupied Huangtukan. On the 20th, our side increased troops and, under the command of Commander Deng, counterattacked the enemy forces in Huangtukan, defeating them, killing their battalion commander Li (Li Shoushan's brother), killing nine rebel soldiers, and wounding more than 30. The enemy retreated to Andong. Huangtukan was recaptured by our army, seizing one pistol and thirteen large guns. Three of our soldiers were wounded. The enemy's northern route consisted of more than 100 Japanese and more than 400 rebel soldiers, who went west from Fengcheng and arrived at Kabaling. Our side deployed heavy troops there for defense, and under the command of Zhang Xiaoqian, Director of Training, Yun and Liang's regiments encountered the enemy troops on the 18th of last month in a fierce battle that lasted half a day. The enemy troops collapsed, killing five enemy soldiers, wounding more than 20, killing one of our soldiers, wounding five, and seizing six large guns. The enemy's central route consisted of 200 Japanese and 400 rebel soldiers, who went west from Andong and contacted our defense forces at Daxiao Lou on the 19th. After fighting for about three hours, the enemy collapsed towards Andong. Furthermore, Dong Rongjiu, Commander-in-Chief of the National Salvation Army, reported to a certain organization in Beiping yesterday that his army had temporarily withdrawn to its original defense on the second day of winter due to lack of supplies and ammunition, and the sudden cold weather, which made it impossible for the soldiers to endure wearing single clothes. The original telegram is recorded as follows: "On the evening of the 26th, I led my troops in three routes to launch a fierce attack on Jinzhou. On the evening of the 29th, Wang's brigade (Wang Yongliang) had broken through the north gate. At dawn on the 30th, the puppet Fengshan Railway Station was also occupied by Cao's brigade (Cao Zhenguo) and Gong Zhongjiu, Li Ronglu, and other troops of our army. The west gate was not captured due to the enemy's firm defense. The headquarters of the division in Jinzhou ordered the entire army to concentrate on defending the north gate, but our soldiers were determined not to fear their machine guns and artillery and continued to charge. The Broadsword Team was the backbone. From the 26th to the 2nd of winter, countless enemy soldiers were cut down. After the loss of the railway station, the enemy dispatched armored trains and a large number of troops to reinforce. Li Ronglu, commander of our First Detachment, and Hou Bifeng, commander of the Second Detachment, then commanded their troops to engage the enemy head-on. Li Shiming, commander of the First Brigade, and Gong Zhongjiu, commander of the Third Detachment, charged the enemy's left flank. Exhibition Commander Zhan Guosi commanded the remaining troops to attack the enemy's right flank. Brigade commanders and detachment commanders personally supervised the troops, and the fighting was fierce, with many enemy soldiers killed. Yesterday, on the afternoon of the 1st, at about 2:00 p.m., the enemy dispatched a large number of planes from the east and west to bomb our various units, causing considerable casualties. And tanks, armored vehicles, etc., covered their infantry, cavalry, and artillery, advancing towards our army, and a fierce battle broke out. That night, the weather suddenly turned cold, and the soldiers were wearing single clothes, making it impossible to endure. In addition, the enemy's mountain artillery and field artillery posed an increasing threat, and our army had been fighting bloodily for six or seven days without stopping, and was extremely exhausted. Our reinforcements were also insufficient, and ammunition was lacking, making it impossible to continue fighting. To avoid losses, I had no choice but to lead the various brigades and detachments to temporarily withdraw to our original defenses on the morning of the 2nd of winter, awaiting the full army to rest and reinforcements to follow. We are determined to fight the violent Japanese to the death, eliminate the puppet state, eradicate the traitors, restore our country, return our mountains and rivers, and sacrifice our lives to repay the country, vowing not to return alive. Respectfully reported by telegram, I hope you will consider this. Dong Rongjiu, Commander-in-Chief of the Northeast People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, bowed on the seal of winter. Results of the Sino-French Border Negotiations in Dongxing

Sino-French Sides Conclude Memorandum

Guangzhou Correspondence: Dongxing, a part of Qinzhou, Guangdong Province, is adjacent to the Gulf of Tonkin in French Indochina, where Chinese and foreigners live together, and disputes often arise. Recently, the provincial government specially set up a French secretary in the Dongxing County Government to handle local negotiations. Since then, minor incidents between Dongxing and the French territory have been resolved locally, unlike in the past when major negotiations would often break out. However, in July of last year, a border case occurred in Dongxing 𥐞 Street, and Zhu Zhaoshen, the diplomatic inspector of the five provinces of China, went to handle it. As a result, the two sides signed the Sino-French Memorandum on the Dongxing Negotiation Case for mutual observance. Until recently, the memorandum has been published. A record is provided below for the reference of those concerned with Sino-French border negotiations. The original memorandum states that one representative, Mr. La Garde, counselor of the French Embassy in China, representing the Vietnamese government, discussed the Dongxing 𥐞 Street border negotiation case with the authorities of Guangdong Province in Guangzhou. Realizing that there were misunderstandings that harmed the interests of both countries, they sincerely wanted to correct this unfortunate situation and further consolidate their mutual relations. Therefore, both parties agreed that the articles of the Sino-Vietnamese Border Police Implementation Regulations signed on May 7, 1896, and the Sino-Vietnamese Border Maintenance of Security Agreement signed on April 13, 1915, should be implemented in accordance with the spirit of honest cooperation and broad mutual implementation. The Sino-French Committee established in Dongxing 𥐞 Street should proceed expeditiously in accordance with the above principles to fulfill its responsibilities. In addition to matters within the scope of its duties, the Sino-French Committee should ㈠ handle any unexpected events that may occur on the border in a friendly and vigorous manner and resolve them locally; ㈡ promote the progress of interests on the border, especially to implement Articles 15 and 16 of the regulations as much as possible, providing long-term passes to local farmers and businessmen in Xing; ㈢ assist in suppressing bandits within their respective territories and without crossing the border in accordance with Articles 18 to 22 of the regulations. Approved and signed by Zhu Zhaoshen, diplomatic inspector of Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, and Guizhou, and Mr. La Garde, counselor of the French Embassy in China, representing French Minister Weier Dian. (November 3rd)

Large Exhibition of Cultural Relics in Beiping

Jointly Held by Eleven Institutions

Raising Funds for Winter Clothing to Relieve the Northeast

Beiping Correspondence: The various academic institutions in Beiping have decided to issue joint tickets from the 6th to the 13th to raise funds for winter clothing to relieve the Northeast. The Palace Museum, the Three Great Halls, Jingshan Park, the Museum of History, the Astronomical Exhibition Hall, the Beiping Research Institute, and the Beiping Library

Page 8

and other eight places, including Tuancheng, will be open to exhibit cultural relics from eleven institutions. The ticket price is only one yuan. With a book of tickets, all places can be visited within eight days. Various academic institutions are now adding珍品 and are busy with arrangements. The general situation is compiled below:

Palace Museum: All珍品 in storage are put on display, and Jingshan Park is also opened at the same time. During the Qianlong era, there was a Western tribute clock with a robot inside. Once started, it could write the eight characters (八方向化九土來王). During the exhibition period, characters will be sold publicly to increase visitors' interest.

Ancient Artifacts Exhibition Hall: Portraits of emperors from the Tang, Song, Yuan, and Ming dynasties are hung in the Three Great Halls. The Mandala built in the Hall of Supreme Harmony during the Kalachakra Tantra Assembly will be preserved as before during the exhibition period for people to view.

Museum of History: Divided into thirteen categories, including excavations, bronze and stone inscriptions, models, and charts. Newly added Dingxing Han Tomb Pottery Horses and Clay Figurines, and many pieces of Yi County Yanxia Capitals Pottery are displayed. In addition, the old collection of Bao Fengkuan, 清 Qianlong's life徐 白齋 所绘 Opera Spring Lantern Hundred 幅, is displayed. The smeared faces and hung beards are different from the current ones. It is not only the treasures of the craftsman's art, but also the changes in the costumes of the opera in the past century. In addition, the Institute of History and Language of the hospital has specially arranged an exhibition room in the museum to display the precious historical materials of the Heavenly Mandate Heavenly Cong Chongde years before the 清 Dynasty entered the customs, and the tortoise shells, bull heads, deer heads, bronzes, jades, stone tools, bone tools, shell tools, white pottery and other items excavated from the Yin Ruins in Anyang over the years. The legacy of the past three thousand years has now been displayed for the people of the old capital to view. The Chinese Society for the Study of Construction has recently paid attention to ancient wooden buildings, so this time it also has an exhibition room in the museum, displaying Jixian's Dule Temple, Baodi's Guangsi Temple, and measured drawings and photos, all of which are famous sites of the Liao Dynasty a thousand years ago. The results of the society's long-term research are specially provided for public viewing this time, which should be welcome to those who care about architecture.

Astronomical Exhibition Hall: Among the ancient astronomical instruments displayed, the Simplified Instrument is a relic of Guo Shoujing of the Yuan Dynasty, and the Celestial Sphere, Rectangular Meridian and Ecliptic Instrument, Horizontal Meridian Instrument, Limitation Instrument, Horizontal Meridian and Latitude Instrument, and Quadrant Instrument are works of Nan Huairen, a Qing Kangxi guest minister. Instruments such as the Jiheng Fuchen Instrument and the Gnomon and Leaking Pot are 精製 during the Qianlong era and are珍品 preserved in science.

Art Exhibition Hall: Huairen Hall, Fuchang Hall, and Yanqing Tower are open at the same time to display rubbings of Beiping ancient temple steles and photographs and drawings of various temples, up to thousands of pieces. Various art珍品 of painting and sculpture are listed.

Beiping Library: A 精室 has been specially opened for disaster relief, displaying fifty types of Song刻 本, fifty types of celebrity transcription books, fifty types of opera, Yongle Dadian Siku Quanshu, Dunhuang scriptures, Hong Yang war maps, Qianlong Southern Tour itinerary maps, etc. The dazzling array is not just for leisurely viewing. The Ancient Artifacts Preservation Committee, in addition to opening Tuancheng to exhibit 玉玉 Buddha 甕, the Northwest Scientific Expedition team specially displays Han wooden slips, bamboo slips, writing brushes, straw raincoats, straw sandals, Tang Dynasty silk paintings and silk shoes, and other cultural relics excavated in Gansu, Xinjiang, and Mongolia in Chengguang Hall over the years, and plans to imitate and sell Han brushes and 玉佛 photos to raise funds to help donations. Bengbu Salt Tide Has Eased

North Salt Public Camp Office Begins Operations

Various Salt Companies Have Also Returned to Their Original State

Miao Qiujie Comes to Bengbu to Find a Solution

Bengbu Correspondence: The North Salt Public Camp Office, run by Huai salt merchants, was vehemently opposed by the salt industry when it was first established in Bengbu, causing a tide. The establishment of the North Salt Camp Office was due to the fact that Huai salt flooded the Bengbu market, and supply exceeded demand, resulting in price drops and抢售. In order to reform the salt administration, two announcements were issued, one allowing salt merchants to directly buy and sell, and the other organizing a Salt Administration Consolidation Committee, which resulted in the production of the North Salt Public Camp Office. The committee also stipulated a number-selling method, such as numbers 1 to 10, which had different salt samples and prices. Customers could choose to buy at their own discretion, and there would be no monopoly or manipulation. However, these fifty-seven salt companies feared that they would be indirectly controlled by the Public Camp Office, indirectly eliminating their brokerage business, and losing the commission (1.9角 per担) they earned from evaluation, introduction, and running errands, resulting in激烈反. In fact, it was just a matter of survival. The salt merchants believed that the North Salt Public Camp Office was established by the salt administration officials to consolidate the salt administration, and its sovereignty was controlled by the salt envoy, which the salt merchants could not participate in. Now, the salt companies are not seeking a proper solution, but are asking the salt envoy to abolish it, and are directly opposing the salt merchants, which is a mistake in the target, and is also very激愤. They have made earnest defenses for the actions of the salt companies, but the salt companies said that the salt merchants were relying on their thick capital to deceive the salt envoy and approved the establishment of the North Salt Public Camp Office, and always believed that they were intentionally monopolizing. The salt merchants and salt administration agencies denied this extremely. Therefore, the salt companies and the salt merchants have been in a stalemate for days. Jin Xiangshao, the Commissioner of the Resident Bengbu Tax Collection Office of the Huaibei Salt Administration Audit Office, felt that he could not remain silent due to his official duties. He reported the demonstration and petition of the salt companies against the North Salt Public Camp to Salt Envoy Miao Qiujie for processing. He also believed that the long-term stalemate between the salt merchants and the salt companies would have a significant impact on the salt administration. Therefore, at 6:00 p.m. on the 4th, he convened a meeting at the Public Security Bureau with more than ten key figures from Fengyang Chief County Mayor Shi Guozhu, Bengbu Public Security Bureau Chief You Kaiyun, and the Bengbu Chamber of Commerce of the Salt Merchants Association and the Salt Industry Association to discuss mediation methods. It was decided that before receiving the explicit order and solution from the Lianghuai Salt Envoy, a compromise method would be determined, that is, the North Salt Public Camp Office would begin operations from the 5th, and the salt companies would also resume work and return to their original state. As for the dispute, they would wait quietly for the Salt Administration to resolve it. All parties were very satisfied with this temporary method. Yesterday (the 5th), the salt industry was operating as usual. This matter seems to have come to an end on the surface, but in the dark, they are still fighting and showing their supernatural powers. In addition, people from Wanbei who are traveling in Bengbu have been卷 入漩, organizing the so-called Wanbei Twenty-One Counties Committee Against the North Salt Public Camp Office, and recommending Yang Yaonan and other twenty-nine people as executive committee members to be responsible for handling negotiations and requesting abolition. The various circles in Bengbu will also establish similar groups against the North Salt Public Camp Office to provide strong support. The salt administration dispute is turning into an expansion trend. This morning (the 6th), Salt Envoy Miao Qiujie specially came to Bengbu by car from Banpu with the British Mr. Pearson, a洋员 from the Audit Office, to resolve this matter. Jin Zhuan, Commissioner of the Salt Administration Tax Collection Office here, and the salt merchants and people from the salt companies received the news in advance and went to the station to meet them. Miao and others got out of the car and went to the Salt Administration Tax Collection Office to stay. In the morning, they convened representatives of various salt companies at the office to talk, and in the afternoon, they convened representatives of salt merchants to talk, separately consulting their opinions and discussing practical and effective compromise methods to completely resolve the problem. The Committee Against the North Salt Public Camp Office, organized by people from Wanbei traveling in Bengbu, also recommended representatives to visit and state their opinions. According to Miao's statement, Lianghuai is an important salt production area in China. In the past, the salt production volume was the highest in Huainan. In the past 20 years, Huainan's production has gradually decreased due to changes in the coastal salt fields, and Huaibei has become the area with the highest salt production. The people of the four provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, Hubei, and Henan mostly rely on this for food. In recent years, due to the decline of river transport, most of the salt is transported by sea and car. The transport is convenient, and the sales are naturally high. The annual salt tax collected is nearly 30 million yuan. Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance pays special attention to the salt administration of Lianghuai. Projects such as dredging rivers and building 坨 are being carried out vigorously. It has been decided to build seven large salt farms in Huainan and twelve in Huaibei with 1.4 million yuan. It is estimated that all projects will be completed by the end of next year at the latest. Wanbei has been a free sales area since the abolition of the 引岸 system nearly 20 years ago. Bengbu is the largest commercial port for selling Huai salt in Wanbei. The highest tax collected was more than 6 million yuan. However, since last year, due to the impact of natural and man-made disasters, the social economy has declined, and people lack the ability to purchase. Therefore, the sales volume of Huai salt is far less than before. The salt tax collected last year was only more than 2 million yuan. And because the transport is free, the number of salt merchants with small capital has increased sharply. The salt transported has therefore become surplus. Since the salt supply exceeds demand, small merchants try to sell it off due to stack rent and discount interest, so the price drops. Other salt merchants also抢售, resulting in a very unstable situation. In order to consolidate the salt administration, the North Salt Public Camp Office was organized to display salt samples and allow customers to purchase them. In order to prevent monopoly and price increases, it is stipulated that a six-month trial period will be implemented. Salt companies are allowed to have tooth licenses and operate as brokers, which are not prohibited by the salt administration officials. However, merchants should not entrust salt companies to intermediate evaluations, and salt companies should not force customers to follow. If customers are willing to entrust salt companies to purchase on their behalf, it is naturally free. I came to Bengbu this time to first convene representatives of salt companies and salt merchants to consult their opinions, so as to use appropriate methods to resolve the dispute. I have no prejudice whatsoever. Judging from Miao's expression, the salt camp dispute may be resolved within a day. (6th)

The Cause of the Japanese Ship Shiraha Maru Running Aground

Carrying over 8,000 Tons of Ore from Daye

Strayed from the Course Leading to Erroneous Impact with Reefs

Zhenjiang Customs, Concerned About Mineral Ore Being Dumped into the River as a Precaution

Has Dispatched Personnel to Monitor and Set a Deadline for Unloading

The Japanese ship Shiraha Maru ran aground at Beixingzhou near Zhenjiang at 7 a.m. on the 3rd. This reporter investigated the Zhenjiang Customs, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha, and Hengda Customs Brokerage yesterday, and found discrepancies from the outside rumors. Originally, the mineral ore produced annually in Daye Ma'anshan, Wuhu and other places in our country contains a lot of iron and the output is quite large. Because there is no perfect iron smelting plant in the country, it is taken away by the Japanese without compensation. In the past, it was customary for commercial ships from that country to carry coal and other goods to Hankou and Yichang, and then transport mineral ore on the return trip, which has been the case for more than a year. Recently, due to the impact of imported goods, Nisshin Kisen Kaisha reluctantly dispatched three ships on the Yangtze River line for route relations, loading daily necessities for Japanese residents. This time, the Tatsuma Kisen Kaisha's Shiraha Maru arrived at Daye at the end of last month with more than 8,000 tons of ore. At 7 a.m. on the 3rd, when it arrived at Beixingzhou, about six miles upstream from Zhenjiang, it ran aground due to the shallow and dry river and straying from the course. It immediately telegraphed for help. Two Japanese warships (Ogi) and (Fuji) have arrived from Nanjing to rescue it. However, because the front of the first cabin is leaning forward, it cannot be towed. Hengda Customs Brokerage, which manages the ship, has reported it to Zhenjiang Customs. Zhenjiang Customs is worried that the Japanese ship will dump mineral ore into the river, blocking the river flow, and has dispatched personnel to station on the ship to monitor and set a deadline for unloading the mineral ore onto other ships. (News Agency)

Wuxi

The Business Tax Bureau Strictly Pursues Tax Payments Since taking office, Xia Zhenlong, the director of the Wuxi Business Tax Bureau, has been earnestly rectifying, and he has been particularly strict in conducting investigations. However, due to the water disaster in Xishan last year and the subsequent Shanghai war, the market has been extremely depressed, and business has been sluggish. Moreover, the business tax rate has suddenly increased by one and a half times this autumn, so many people are unable to pay. However, the bureau is very strict in collecting payments, and most people have reluctantly paid the spring and summer seasons first. However, industries such as rice, money, cotton yarn, flour, sauce and wine, grain, rickshaw, and coal have either paid the brokerage tax or have special business circumstances, and have failed to declare on time. They have successively requested Director Xia to consider the difficulties of the merchants and consider both tax revenue and business conditions. Yesterday, he specially reported the above-mentioned industries to County Magistrate Lu and summoned the leaders of each industry to a meeting to discuss and urge them to resolve the matter as soon as possible. The industry directors stated their difficulties in person and promised to discuss a solution immediately. An Old Farmer Committed Suicide by Hanging Due to Injustice In Caozhuangli, Changbang River, Zhangjingqiao, Huai Shangshi, the 7th district of the county, Xu, the wife of Wang Renquan, a villager, was nearly forty years old, naturally fierce and specializing in gossiping, hence the nickname "long-tongued woman." On the 4th of this month, Xu suddenly falsely accused Chen Jinfu, the neighbor on the right, of stealing manure, and scolded him all day long for two days and one night without rest. However, Chen Jinfu was sixty-two years old, honest by nature, and felt deeply wronged by this false accusation, so he became disgusted with the world. He hanged himself in his room early in the morning the day before yesterday without anyone knowing. When his wife discovered it, he had already died of suffocation. His wife was extremely saddened and cried bitterly. Later, she reported it to the Township Office and requested to appeal the injustice. The village chiefs Wang Zhihe and Wang Sanyuan, among others, came forward to mediate and ordered Wang Renquan to pay 40 yuan in funeral expenses as a settlement. A case of a life lost due to stealing manure was thus resolved.

Strict Prohibition of Private Issuance of Cash Chips The shops such as Dingfeng Liu Xinchang in Meicun Town, the 10th district, privately manufactured cash chips, which were popular in the market and disrupted the financial order. The county government strictly ordered Yuan Yongtang, the district head of the district, to ban them. District Head Yuan issued a notice ordering each household to prohibit them all at the end of last month and to collect them on their own. Unexpectedly, the shops still disobeyed in secret, and cash chips were still rampant in the market. After District Head Yuan learned of this, he went to the Meicun Town Office with assistant Qin Zhicang yesterday morning and summoned the town head Chen Shengshan and the shopkeepers of each cash chip issuing shop to the office, urging them to prepare cash as soon as possible to redeem the cash chips outside. He also granted a grace period of half a month, allowing them to be collected in full by the 15th of this month. The shopkeepers were ordered to hand over the unissued cash chips and burn them first. After all the chips were collected by the 15th, they would be burned for the second time. Soon, the shopkeepers complied with the order and handed over the cash chips stored in their shops, totaling about 200,000 wen, piled up in front of the town office and burned together under the supervision of District Head Yuan.

Changshu

Schools in the Fourth District Petition the County Bureau Educational funding in our county has been in arrears for eight or nine months. The principals of each school all have the lament of a clever housewife. However, the education authorities, because of the precedent of arrears, do not try to plan, but instead issue half a period every one or two months to deal with the situation. Now, the schools in the fourth school district, because they see that the arrears are huge and difficult to cope with, gathered at their respective villages the day before yesterday to discuss solutions. As a result, it was decided to send twelve representatives to the city on the 5th to petition the Education Bureau to release the arrears. The Director of the Education Bureau, Yu Cheng, said that one period, half old and half new, could be released between the 15th and 20th of this month, and there was no guarantee beyond that. The representatives, unable to find a satisfactory solution, went to the County Government in the afternoon to petition. The Matricide Case Will Be Retried in Suzhou In the autumn of the 17th year of the Republic of China, Cai Yizhi, a gentleman from Baoben Street in this county, conspired to seize property, and colluded with rickshaw puller Zeng Zeng, his wife Jin, and his concubine Li, to strangle his adoptive mother Cai Qu to death on the night of October 10th. Subsequently, Qu's son-in-law Weng Qiaosheng and others sued the county. After the county examined and verified the facts, Cai Yizhi and the two rickshaw pullers were sentenced to death, and the wife and concubine were sentenced to life imprisonment. Cai and others refused to accept the sentence and repeatedly appealed to the High Court and the Supreme Court. After several years of transfer, the Supreme Court finally ruled on the matter last month and sent it back to the High Court for retrial. Now, the High Court has scheduled the retrial in Suzhou on the 8th of this month. The rickshaw puller Qian Zeng and concubine Li have already passed away. It is not yet known whether there will be any changes during the retrial.

Zhenjiang

Registration Deadline Set for Land in Dakoumen The Zhenjiang County Land Bureau stated that since houses are currently being demolished and roads are being built in the Dakoumen area, all locations should comply with the regulations and apply for registration. Despite repeated announcements urging compliance, the residents have still been hesitant and have not complied with the regulations. The bureau issued another announcement yesterday, setting a deadline for the landowners to comply with the registration within one week. No applications will be accepted after the deadline.

Yangzhou

Inmates of the Reformatory Escaped and Injured a Policeman At the Reformatory for Vagrants, yesterday afternoon at dinner time, seven vagrants including Li Jintai, Tian Mazi, He Zhengcai, Shen Jiren, Tian Jintang, and Pan Yiqing took advantage of the institution's unpreparedness and rushed out, injuring the gatekeeper Yang Yu. The institution's staff caught He Zhengcai and He Guocai. The case has been reported to the Public Security First Branch for assistance in a strict search.

Imposter Posing as a Committee Member of the Department of Civil Affairs Arrested The Public Security First Branch of Jiangdu arrested a young military officer wearing a yellow woolen uniform last night. He identified himself as Wu Tie'an, a secret investigator of opium for the Department of Civil Affairs, and accompanied by the resident patrol officer of the bureau, went to designated locations to investigate and arrest opium and gambling activities. However, nothing was found. Later, the resident patrol officer suspected his behavior and feared that he was an imposter. He was immediately arrested and sent to the headquarters. Under interrogation, he confessed that he was indeed an imposter and also admitted that he went by the name of Tushan and that he had friends Su Pinshan and Xu Jiasong, who lived in Kangshan in the city. The bureau then dispatched Inspector Lang to lead the police to arrest them together. A suitcase was found in Wu's residence (No. 29, Dalu Hostel), as well as Wu Tie'an's business card, wooden seals of Qian Jiaqi of the Third Section of the Jiangsu Department of Civil Affairs, symbols such as Wu Xiang, the deputy adjutant of the 264th Brigade of the 88th Division, and the deputy adjutant of the General Political Training Department of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, and two forged instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs. All of them were sent to the headquarters for investigation and prosecution.

Nantong

Joint Levee Protection by Counties in Jiangbei In recent years, the course of the Yangtze River has changed, and the erosion in the Jiangbei area has been severe. The Nantong Construction Bureau believes that the levee protection project is huge and cannot be undertaken by one county alone. It has submitted a request to the Construction Department to order the counties along the river in Jiangbei to organize a joint levee protection association to jointly raise construction funds. In addition, the provincial government will provide subsidies according to the example of the Jiangnan levee project to facilitate the progress of the project.

Elementary and Secondary School Teachers Petition for Salaries Salaries for elementary and secondary school teachers throughout Nantong County have been in arrears for seven months. On the 6th, more than 50 representatives of male and female teachers went to the county government to petition for their salaries. County Magistrate Zhang promised to instruct the Finance Bureau to find a way to allocate funds.

Inspection Team of the Reclamation Zone Arrives in Tong The inspection team of the Jiangbei Reclamation Zone is conducting an on-site investigation. All members of the team gathered in Tong and traveled along the coast north to Rugao, Taixian, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Funing. Pi Zuoqiong, a representative of the Ministry of Industry, arrived in Tong on the 5th. He Yushu, Li Mingyang, Miao Bin, and others arrived in the port from Shanghai within seven days. Local communities prepared to welcome them.

Rugao

Robbery Case at Gao'er Bridge At the Shi surname chicken shop in Gao'er Bridge, Shizhuang, yesterday around 11 p.m., more than a dozen bandits suddenly came, broke into the door, tied up the shop owner, and beat him severely. They robbed more than 100 yuan of chicken money and many pieces of clothing. When the Shizhuang Security Corps heard the news and rushed to the scene, the bandits had already fled far away.

Gaoyou

Inspection Committee Conducts Second Inspection of the Embankment Project The Jiangbei Canal Embankment was inspected in July by the Jiangbei Canal Project Inspection Committee, which was jointly organized by the Jiangsu Provincial Government and various agencies. Personnel were dispatched to inspect it separately. At that time, many sections of the embankment project had collapsed and were unloaded. The responsible persons have rebuilt the projects, and the various projects have now been completed one after another. Inspection Committee members Dong Bochun and others conducted a second inspection. The committee members departed from Qingjiang on the 1st to inspect the Huaipi section of the project. On the 4th, they inspected the east and west embankments from Jieshou to Dangjunlou. This morning (the 5th), they inspected the four breaches outside the north gate of this city and the east and west embankments of the Lincheng section, completing the inspection at 11 a.m. They then traveled south to inspect the projects at Erjia and Laisheng'an.

Kerosene Boat Robbed and Burned by Bandits Two kerosene boats belonging to a kerosene company in Zhenjiang were transporting kerosene to Qingjiang for distribution inside the county lake last night around 10 p.m. They were suddenly encountered by two bandit boats carrying more than a dozen bandits, each armed with guns. They jumped onto the kerosene boats and searched them extensively, finding a total of 80 foreign dollars. The bandits still thought it was not enough and carried the kerosene onto the bandit boats. Unexpectedly, they broke the oil tank, and kerosene splashed on the lamp and caught fire immediately. The bandits immediately escaped on their original boats. It is said that the losses were quite large.

Party Department Raises Donations to Aid the Righteous Army The County Party Department of this county, yesterday (the 4th), decided through an executive committee meeting to appoint Huang Songtao and Chen Jiarang to raise donations from all walks of life to aid the Northeast Volunteer Army.

Pinghu

Water Police Detachment Arrests Robbery Suspects The homes of Wang Chunrong and Wang Shanmin in Zhang Doufang, Xinjie Town, were suddenly robbed on the night of the 28th of last month. The loss of silver dollars and clothing was very large. The next day, they reported to the Water Police Third Detachment stationed in the town. Upon receiving the report, Detachment Commander Zhang Hengqing immediately dispatched a senior police officer to conduct a careful and secret investigation. Yesterday, they found clues and arrested four robbery suspects: Shi Qiancang, Xie Shengwu, Chen Youyu, and Li Fangrong. After interrogation and confessions, a document was prepared and sent to the county for legal action. Investigating Judge Dismissed for Murder Case Zhang Xiaoda of Guangchen Township was plotted to death by Yuan Xiangqing and others. He was arrested by Investigating Judge Song during his tenure and sent to prison pending investigation. After Qu Shizuo took over as investigating judge, the victim's family submitted five petitions requesting investigation, but they were all ignored. There was a rumor of an 800 yuan bribe. Unexpectedly, during this time, Investigating Judge Qu Shizuo ordered Yuan Xiangqing to be released on bail. The victim's family was in an uproar and immediately complained to the High Court by listing the facts through the aggrieved Zhang Sanguan (the deceased's brother). The president of the court was greatly angered upon reading the petition and ordered a strict investigation. First, Investigating Judge Qu Shizuo was dismissed, and the original file was sent to the court for review.

Large Numbers of Refugees Pass Through Eight refugee boats from Hunan arrived at Datongqiao Town in this county the day before yesterday, with a total of 200 people. They spent lavishly and behaved extravagantly, causing disturbances along the way. Upon hearing the news, the local Security Corps led the entire team of soldiers to patrol and strictly guard against them. The next day, they raised travel expenses and gave them to the refugees before they left for Zhongdai.

Hangzhou

Lu Dipin's Condition Slightly Improves Lu Dipin, the chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government, suffered a stroke and fainted at a banquet for the Fifth Provincial Representative Conference the other day. He was then helped to the secretary-general's office and injected with medicine by a Western doctor for emergency treatment, and then regained consciousness. He has been resting in the chairman's office for days due to his serious illness. He also extended an invitation to Chinese medicine practitioner He Gongdan for diagnosis and treatment. Because the chairman suffered from hyperemia that has not yet healed, the provincial government specially sent clerk Li Xiyi to Shanghai on the 6th to invite Director Le of the Red Cross Hospital to Hangzhou for diagnosis and treatment. Lu's condition has slightly improved. His hiccups stopped at 1 a.m. this morning (the 7th). He had some bread in the morning, but he is still dizzy, his hands are numb, and he hates noise. If his condition improves further during the day, he will need to go to Lingyin Temple to recuperate and treat his illness.

Hefei

Entire City's Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Shut Down Due to Excessive Taxes The 80-plus tobacco and alcohol businesses in the Hefei urban area have been subjected to a unified tax collection for the urban area and suburbs for more than ten years, with monthly revenues of only a hundred-plus yuan. The current contract holder for the urban area and suburbs of the tax collection bureau suddenly increased the tax amount tenfold. Those who were responsible for collecting three yuan of alcohol tax were increased to thirty yuan, and those who were responsible for one yuan of tobacco tax were increased to ten-plus yuan. This was already unanimously opposed. However, yesterday, the tax collection bureau investigated the goods in Yixingshun Tobacco Shop on Beirujie Street and had a verbal conflict, arresting the shop owner Li Jingbao and sending him to the county government for detention, causing a great uproar. On the 3rd, all the tobacco and alcohol shops in the city were closed, and a petition was submitted to the head office for relief.

Major Fire Outside the West Gate There has been no rain here for several months, and the drought is extreme. The rivers and wells are dry, and the two wheat crops cannot be planted safely. The farmers are afraid of famine. Unexpectedly, at noon on the 2nd, a fire suddenly broke out at the Xu surname house next to Shdashan on Erlijie Street outside the West Gate. At that time, the south wind was strong, and the north and south streets were both affected. Moreover, there was no water for rescue, so the situation became more severe. The Liuhe Automobile Station was also burned down. Fortunately, the military police dismantled the connecting houses on all sides and extinguished the fire after two hours. A total of 14 households and more than 140 houses were burned down. After 7 p.m., a haystack behind Pingliang Villa on Gulou Street in the city caught fire again for unknown reasons. Fortunately, it was in a busy market, and military police and water dragons all arrived to put out the fire, and only three houses were burned.

Education News

Important News

Central Talk Association Decides to Severely Punish Beixin

Nanhua to Cease Publication and Authors to Be Punished

Improve Primary and Secondary School Curriculum and Teaching Materials

Nanjing, 7th The Central Talk Association was held on the morning of the 7th. The attendees were Ju Zheng, Gu Mengyu, Chen Guofu, Shi Ying, He Qingqin, Song Peide, Huang Musong, Chu Minyi, Ding Chaowu, Shao Yuanchong, Miao Peicheng, Wang Qi, and other twenty-plus people. Chairman Ju Zheng discussed the various proposals, and the results are as follows:

(1) In the past, there were many shortcomings in the curriculum and teaching materials of primary and secondary schools. It is imperative to improve them in the future. Recently, the central government decided to organize a committee, hire many educators in the country, and based on the education proposals accepted by the previous central governments, conduct a detailed research to formulate a practical implementation plan and submit it to the Third Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee for deliberation and decision, so as to achieve the principle of rationalizing education and cultivating healthy citizens.

(2) Regarding the representatives' request to punish the bookstore that published words insulting Islam, after discussion, it was stated that during the national crisis, one should not publish words that harm national feelings. It was advocated that the Beixin Bookstore should be severely punished, Nanhua Literature and Art should be suspended, and the author of this article should be punished according to law. In the future, any publication is prohibited from publishing words that provoke national feelings. Efforts should be made to improve the teaching materials of various schools so as to integrate the differences between ethnic groups. The Propaganda Committee and the Executive Yuan will be responsible for handling this matter separately.

(3) Recommend Committee Member Zhou Qigang to attend the next Commemorative Week to report.

Nanjing, 7th The Ministry of Education recently ordered the provincial education departments to announce that the short-term elementary school textbooks compiled by the ministry have been printed by the Zhonghua Book Company. If these textbooks are needed, they can be ordered directly from the book company.

Jiangsu Province's Scout Inspection Competition

The Jiangsu Provincial Scout Grand Jamboree was held on the 6th with a formal grand inspection. The weather was very cold that day, and the cold wind was piercing, but the healthy men and women were still wearing short clothes and were as energetic as usual. At 7:30 in the morning, they departed from the campsite outside the South Gate, marched in formation to the Municipal Stadium in the city. It is estimated that there were 10,000 spectators at the venue. The details of the inspection are described below.

Inspection Personnel Representatives of the Central Party Headquarters: Ye Chucang; representatives of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek: He Yingqin, Vice President of the Chinese Scout General Association; Committee members of the Central Executive Committee: Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Luo Jialun, Yu Jingtang; representatives of the Military Advisory Council: Tan Jiajun, Zhou Shaoqi; representatives of the Preparatory Office of the Chinese Scout General Association: Teng Jie; Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government: Gu Zhutong; Director of the Department of Education: Zhou Fohai; Committee members of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Headquarters: Ma Yuanfang, Yang Xingqin, He Weibin, Zhang Gongren, Cao Minghuan, Ge Jianshi, etc.

Inspection Ceremony (1) Opening; (2) Playing music and raising the flag; (3) Singing the Party song; (4) Paying the highest tribute to the national flag, the Party flag, and the portrait of the Supreme Leader; (5) Chairman respectfully reads the will of the Premier; (6) Chairman's report; (7) Admonitory speech; (8) Cheers and completion of the ceremony.

Inspection Situation After the members of the Central Committee took the command platform, all the Scouts went around the entire venue for a week, first performing a procession. The Jiangsu Provincial Government, Public Security Bureau, and Military Band led the way in front, the music and steps corresponded with each other. Each team raised their hands to show respect as they walked in front of the command platform. This took a quarter of an hour. Next, they performed the farewell ceremony. Each inspection committee member patrolled around the platform for a week, and then performed health exercises. Song Tieming, recommended by the , conducted the platform crowd model, and each Scout performed each exercise one by one. The movements were , clear, and . Everyone watched the results of the exercise, and then the members相gave instructions.

Chairman's Report Chairman Gu Zhutong reported that the Scouts of Jiangsu Province have been established for more than 20 years. In 1924, they participated in the World Scout Jamboree. In 1930, they participated in the National Scout Grand Review, and their results were not behind. I hope that all Scouts will take the Three People's Principles as the highest principle, have an independent spirit, pure thoughts, and not be tempted by other , noble character, and not be bound by any environment. In addition to personal freedom, protect the freedom of the group. Deeply understand yourself and make it your mission to wash away national shame.

Commission Members' Admonitory Speech First, Central Representative Ye Chulun delivered a speech, hoping that all Scouts would bring out all their talents, take on great responsibilities, and be models for the whole country, so as to win glory for the nation. He Yingqin's admonitory speech: The Scouts of Jiangsu Province account for one-third of the country, which can be said to be second to none. I hope that all of you children will strictly abide by the eleven rules and disciplines that Scouts should have, and in the spirit of Premier Sun Yat-sen's creation of the Three People's Principles, embrace a love for the people, love for the country, and love for humanity, and be prepared to serve the group and society. Now that the people and mountains of the Northeast have fallen into the hands of the , I hope everyone will work hard to avenge their country and revenge. Luo Jialun's admonitory speech said that China's position is dangerous, not afraid of the oppression of imperialism and foreign soldiers, but only afraid that the nation will not rise up and not be aggressive. The nation should have a spirit of unity, not rely on the tangible army, but rely on the intangible army to fight. Every soldier should be a healthy citizen, and every citizen must be a healthy soldier. When the spirit is put into practice, even three thousand Scouts can抵 three hundred thousand strong enemies. I hope everyone will be a healthy member of the nation. Finally, Teng Jie and Zhang Gongren successively delivered admonitory speeches. Commission Members' Inscriptions The this Grand Scout Jamboree will be publishing a commemorative album, and the members were specially invited to write inscriptions. He Yingqin wrote: (Reviving the Chinese nation and consolidating the spirit is the responsibility of our Scouts.) Ye Chucang wrote: (Realizing the Three People's Principles and completing the National Revolution.) Luo Jialun wrote: (Every soldier should be a healthy citizen, and every citizen should be a healthy soldier.) Chen Lifu wrote: (Sacrifice freedom and contribute ability.)

After the admonitory speeches, everyone sang the Scout song, cheered, threw their hats, and the meeting adjourned.

Bridge Building

Central Government to Formulate Overall Education Reform Plan

Political Conference to Deliberate at Length Before Submitting to the Third Plenary Session; Central Committee Members Discuss Three Failures of Current Chinese Schools and Social Education

Nanjing, 7th Dispatch: This morning, at the Central Government Discussion Meeting, Central Committee members expressed three opinions on education reform: 1. Today, not only higher education has failed in China, but also elementary education and social education are nominal and lack substance or a unified plan. Therefore, the general public has a very weak concept of the country, leading some to willingly become traitors and accomplices. If social education were well-managed, such things would not happen. 2. In the past, in addition to inappropriate education systems or policies, many textbooks used in primary and secondary schools today are also unsuitable for the needs of the times. In the future, strict review or revision is necessary. 3. Current popular movies, dramas, novels, poems, and other content rarely improve society or stimulate national spirit, with most being works of love or mythology. This is directly related to social education and must be considered in the overall plan for education reform. As a result of the discussions, the committee members proposed submitting these opinions to the Political Conference for a comprehensive plan and assigning several additional members from the Executive Committee to discuss it together within two weeks. Once the overall plan is finalized, it will be submitted to the Second Plenary Session of the Executive Committee for a decision.

Local News

Chinese Universities Joint Association

Executive Committee Meeting on December 2nd or 9th

Since the Chinese Universities Joint Association Preparatory Committee was established following the resolution of the Higher Education Discussion Meeting during the summer vacation of this year, it has spared no effort in carrying out association affairs. Today, a third Executive Committee meeting was held at the China Association. Attendees included Hu Duanxing (Jiaotong University), Huang Zhaozhao (Nanjing University), Dai Che (Zhonghua Vocational School), Yuan Huai (Renmin University, representing Gao Zhisheng), and Li Yifang (Jinling Women's College, represented by Li Zhaohuan). The meeting was chaired by Gao Zhisheng, with Li Zhaohuan serving as secretary. A. Reporting Items: 1. Representatives from Jiaotong University reported on the National Higher Education Problems Discussion Association. A total of 500 copies were printed, costing 52 yuan. 2. Representatives from various universities reported that various universities had inquired about the association's constitution, seal carving, letterhead, envelopes, etc. B. Discussion Items: 1. Proposal to distribute the report of the National Higher Education Problems Discussion Meeting. It was decided to distribute two copies to each public and private technical college and above. 2. Proposal to distribute the draft regulations of the Chinese Universities Joint Association. It was decided to mimeograph the draft regulations and include a letter explaining and soliciting opinions from various schools. 3. Proposal to carve the association's seal, letterhead, and envelopes. It was decided to proceed as planned. 4. Jiangnan University Football Tournament to Open Soon

Starts on the 19th of This Month

The Jiangnan Universities Athletic Association's football championship game will begin on the 19th of this month and will be held every Saturday. Regulations and orders have been established and compiled as follows:

1. Using a round-robin system.

2. The winning team in each game gets two points, the losing team gets zero points, and a tie gets one point each. If two teams have the same total score, another game will be scheduled, and the date will be determined by the football committee.

3. The game rules will follow the football rules of the National Games.

4. The referees will be invited by the host team and must have the consent of the visiting team.

5. If the field is not suitable due to rain or force majeure, the game may be rescheduled. The host team must notify the visiting team and obtain their consent. The make-up game must be held before December 30th.

6. If a team does not appear on the field to play within fifteen minutes of the scheduled game time, it will be considered a forfeit. However, if an accident occurs en route that causes a delay, it will not be counted.

7. The winning team must notify the chairman of the football committee of the game results within three days.

8. The list of players must be sent to the chairman of the football committee for review by the review committee before November 19th.

9. Schedule (each game starts at 2:30 PM)

November

19th Fudan at Chizhi, Central at Guanghua, Jiaotong at Daxia

20. Daxia at Jinan, Fudan at Central, Chizhi at Jiaotong

December

3rd Daxia at Guanghua, Jinan at Chizhi, Jiaotong at Central

10th Daxia at Fudan, Chizhi at Guanghua, Central at Jinan

17th Jiaotong at Fudan, Chizhi at Central, Guanghua at Jinan

18. Guanghua at Jiaotong, Fudan at Jinan, Central at Daxia

19. Jiaotong at Jinan, Fudan at Guanghua, Chizhi at Daxia

National Sports Advancement Association Announces Changes to Women's Basketball Rules Summary

The National Sports Advancement Association announced yesterday the changes to the 1932-1933 Women's Basketball Rules as follows:

1. The center circle diameter is increased to two feet (previously two feet).

2. Holding the ball for more than ten seconds during a free throw is considered a violation (previously a technical foul).

3. Legal defense is not limited to the vertical plane, as long as there is no physical contact.

4. All shots are counted as one point (previously those counted as one point were counted as two points).

Peculiar Changes in the Securities and Bond Market Yesterday

｜Increased by 80 to 150 Cents Compared to Previous Days｜

｜Turnover Reached Over 5,800,000 Yuan｜

Yesterday (the 7th), the situation of various bond markets at the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange was as follows: most spot transactions opened, with a turnover of 37,000 yuan, of which 15,000 yuan for the 1929 Customs bonds was relatively large, with the rest being only a few thousand yuan. The forward market saw a strong rebound, and the market sentiment was lively. Trading volume was far greater than last weekend, with 2,100,000 yuan in the morning session and over 3,700,000 yuan in the afternoon session, totaling 5,825,000 yuan. Among them, salt tax bonds accounted for about 1,500,000 yuan, 1931 Customs bonds and consolidated tax bonds each accounted for 800,000 to 900,000 yuan, disbandment bonds, 1929 Customs bonds, and Relief bonds each accounted for 400,000 to 500,000 yuan, and other bonds remained relatively stable. As for the trend of various bond prices, there was a sudden and peculiar change, with a very sharp increase compared to previous days. However, there has been no major development in the overall environment of the bond market. Although the domestic and international situation seems better, there has been no obvious progress. The biggest reason is that those with a long-term vision in the market believe that the future is quite promising, thus making huge investments and aggressively buying in. The attitude of major players is no longer as indifferent as before. This is why bond prices have been rising recently, with demand constantly exceeding supply. Yesterday's continued firm trend was also due to this. It was observed that various prices rose steadily in each trading session, resulting in an increase of 80 to 145 cents compared to the previous day. The market situation was particularly good for a time.

Flour Prices Suddenly Soar Yesterday

｜Short Covering and Major Factories Buying In｜

Prices for foreign wheat were only one dime. At the opening of the session, prices for the current month were weak, but market sentiment for December was good, and prices rose by one cent, causing prices to rise steadily in subsequent sessions. Short covering was particularly urgent for a time. Major factories were said to be buying in to maintain flour prices, but smaller factories were still selling. Due to the cheap market prices, non-industry customers also bought a lot, so prices for each month rose steadily. When the afternoon session opened, major factories were said to be buying in regardless of delivery date, so the market situation for each month was boosted again, even better than the morning session. As for the price of foreign wheat, it was heard that British and American firms were quoting 3.248 yuan, while Japanese merchants were only quoting 3.245 yuan. Although there were rumors that foreign wheat would be subject to import duties, this was a matter of human intervention, and the low global prices should be viewed separately. As a result, the price for the current month rose by 1.5 cents compared to the previous week, the price for December rose by 3.75 cents, the price for January rose by 3.25 cents, the price for February rose by 2.25 cents, the price for March rose by 2 cents, and the price for April rose by 1.75 cents.

Forward Wheat Rebounds Strongly

Yesterday, the forward wheat market showed a consistent firm upward trend for each month in both the morning and afternoon sessions. The price of foreign wheat rebounded by one dime, and sellers in the market naturally disappeared. Moreover, because the attitude of major factories was unpredictable, speculators became hesitant. The number of chips this year was actually not many, and it was easy to rise if a few people pushed up the price. It was rumored that merchants from Guangdong intended to speculate, and all sessions saw buying in, resulting in a rapid rebound in near and far futures. However, this situation was purely a temporary relationship between supply and demand, and the future cannot be based on this. As a result, the price for the current month remained unchanged, the prices for December and January each rose by four cents compared to the previous week, the price for March rose by five cents, and the price for April rose by six cents.

Since resuming work, the silk factory has seen a daily increase in the production of raw silk, silk cocoons, and by-products. Therefore, the shipment of raw silk and other goods to Shanghai is not uncommon. Yesterday, a Shanghai-Wuxi freight train transported another 320 dan of double cocoons to Shanghai, where they were unloaded and prepared for processing.

Foreign Tea Market is Slightly Quiet

Yesterday, the local foreign tea market was quiet due to the horse racing by Western merchants. British firms only had half-day transactions. Only Baitou, Zhuang Ruichang, Yulong and other places, and China Tea Company, purchased Zhenmei, Zhenmei, Emei, Gongxi, Xiamei and other goods, totaling 460 boxes. Market prices did not fluctuate much. However, according to general news, sources in Yantong claimed that tea sales in the Moroccan market have gradually started to move. It is expected that the market will be active after the Western merchants' autumn races.

Large Number of Pieces of Western Suits and Flannel Were Traded

Western suits, top pieces and flannels, have recently seen a large appetite from Western clothing tailors. Due to the gradually cooling weather, actual sales are in demand. The current order business of door-front stores has increased sharply. In particular, the newly popular Hanling Peng Sportex four-bubble Dex GofteX Kauff's Dex Sprioghon and other three types of Western suits and top-pieces flannels, which have a good shape and are selling well. Seaside Western Clothing Shops all have considerable orders, and their trend is better than other wool fabrics.

Coal: Shanxi Coal Continues to Rise by Half a Yuan

Yesterday, the market price of Shanxi white coal rose by five cents per ton, so the current selling price must be 15.75 yuan per ton. Red Qi white coal and Mark white coal were therefore also raised by 2.5 cents.

Free Talk

Quotations of Ma Xiangbo, a 93-Year-Old

Response Regarding Quotations

Leshan Hall recently received a letter from Macau, which stated: | (To Elder Xiangbo. Respectfully, I have admired your quotations in Shen Bao for some time. Your rich experience, clear understanding of worldly affairs, and sophisticated knowledge of human relationships are indeed extraordinary for an elder. | Yesterday, I read a sentence in your quotations, "(Only sincerity lasts forever)," which I would like to match. I, with my humble skills, have composed a matching sentence. I wonder if there is anything worth considering? If my trivial skill is unsuitable, it does not matter. I hope you will correct it, which would be my pleasure. | Respectfully, your servant, Lin Andeng.

Four sentences are extracted: 1. "Filial piety should be admired for a thousand years"; 2. "The great path cannot be abandoned for a moment"; 3. "Do not leave behind a thousand years of regret for a misstep"; 4. "Never forget to show kindness at any moment." The rest have been deleted. After reading this letter, Elder Xiang said: "(It would be best to collect Wang Xizhi's posthumous works and use the original sentences to match. I once tried to compose the sentence (Who mourns that fleeting scenes all return to nothingness) to match (Only sincerity lasts forever). Why not publish the original text and let the public ponder it?)

In this case, I have no choice but to spend half a day copying Mr. Yu Youren's calligraphy to share with the public and wait for the next public announcement. |

Eulogy to Civil War启沃

For the sake of preserving peace in East Asia and maintaining world peace, Chinese soldiers would rather endure a bellyful of anger and internal strife than rashly provoke an international war. Even losing thousands of miles of territory is of no concern. This "sacrificing everything for the greater good" attitude and dedication to peace can only be found in Chinese soldiers. Nobel Peace Prize, is it in China? Is it in China?

Having experienced disaster and banditry, the common people are in a miserable state, barely human. They cannot find work, and they are starving but not dying. Since they are useless in this world, it would be better to wipe them out with a single cannon blast. The battlefield is full of stray dogs, saving the cost of coffins, which would save a sum of money. Moreover, according to eugenics, these lower-class people should not be bred as much as important people, as it affects the nation's physical health. Failing to eliminate them early will lead to regret.

The noble meaning of civil war is thus and so!

Gaotai Ge Fair in Northern Cixi

— Chi Fo

| Entertainment without forgetting to save the country?

Of course. When Beiping holds the Kalachakra Dharma Assembly to pray for national peace, then the countryside | Cixi North Township Shanbei | holding the Gaotai Ge fair is also a way to pray for national peace. Shanbei in Northern Cixi is located by the sea and backed by mountains. The customs are strong. Since the early Qing Dynasty, there has been a tradition of welcoming gods and holding fairs every year in the third month of the lunar calendar. Some say that the Ming Dynasty was destroyed by the Manchus, and the survivors were deeply resentful. They used the fair to imply revolution. The god they welcome is said to be the East Peak Emperor, but in reality, it is Emperor Huaizong of the Ming Dynasty. Therefore, the fair in the third month is to commemorate the day of Emperor Huaizong's martyrdom. | In Eastern Zhejiang, every family inserts willow branches on Qingming Festival, which also means summoning souls. Also, during Thanksgiving, paper horses of (All Saints of the Southern Dynasty) are offered. The people of Ningbo like to chant the Sun Sutra and devoutly believe in Zhu Tian Bodhisattva. All are good evidence of anti-Qing and restoration of the Ming. | Although Lu You's poem says: Once home, I invite the women of the western neighbors, to watch the god fair on the bridge tomorrow.) Fairs were already popular in the Song Dynasty, but our fairs in Eastern Zhejiang have a special meaning.

This Gaotai Ge fair in Northern Cixi has not been held for twenty-nine years. The fair is nothing rare. The banners and ceremonial guards are not very characteristic compared to the Jiangwan fair. However, the Gaotai Ge is as high as thirty-three feet and is carried by seventy-two people. | Twenty-four people are in a group, and they take turns carrying it. | The stage does not use children dressed as theatrical figures but is strung together by adults. It is said that each Gaotai Ge costs as much as ten thousand foreign dollars. The entire fair is divided into fourteen communities, and each community is funded by the people of each fort. There are a total of fourteen Gaotai Ge, and the expenses are already considerable. Moreover, the places where the Gaotai Ge passes, although not encountering mountains to open mountains and encountering rivers to build bridges, must demolish obstacles such as eaves and towers without resistance. The roads should be temporarily built by the people of each fort, about two feet wide, and filled very smoothly. I think, why is the Gaotai Ge unique in the Shanbei fair? Perhaps there is a special history. There is a small city in Shanbei called (Guanhaiwei), which was built during the Ming Dynasty to defend against Japanese pirates. Because it is located near the sea, Japanese pirates often came to harass it. This Gaotai Ge may have been used to scout Japanese pirates, and the fair was a practice of military preparations for the people. Otherwise, although other fairs have Gaotai Ge, why are they not thirty-three feet high?

On the 5th, 6th, and 7th of this month, the Gaotai Ge fair will be held in Northern Cixi. There will be crowds of people and a lively atmosphere! If the friends who watch the fair remember the story of resisting Japanese pirates, practice military affairs while farming, then they can be said to be (entertaining without forgetting to save the country). | This fair was originally prohibited by the county magistrate, but later, a powerful person supported it, and the county sent troops to protect it. It is heard that the first community is called (Zhongshan Association), and the god they carry is of course Mr. Zhongshan.

.

Contradiction

— Wo

On one hand, they sing the praises of (expert government) (expert administration), while on the other hand, a dentist is the county magistrate, a soldier is the chairman, a geologist is the education leader, and a natural scientist is the Minister of Communications.

X X X

(Long-term resistance) and (punishing pseudo-organizations) are slogans that we are tired of hearing, yet there are no traces of our armed comrades outside the pass. Those rushing between the Black Mountains and White Waters are still the volunteer soldiers fighting the enemy in single clothes, receiving verbal assistance from the great men.

Old and Faded Pearls Are Worthless

— Ke Ding'an

| How should young people be? |

The happiest golden age of life is before the age of ten! However, I should declare in advance that what is recorded now is for people of the same stage as me. Others with (super) or (special) abilities are, of course, not included in this example.

After you pass your tenth anniversary, this is the first major turning point in life. Before, you were at home or at school. Your parents or teachers probably always thought you were too young and did not restrain you very much. But after you turn ten, your parents or teachers will urge you even more. Indeed, in these years, there must be adequate preparations for entering school or business. This is the foundation. If the foundation is not solid, even if the grand building on top is beautifully built, it will eventually collapse.

XX XX XX

Young people over the age of twenty are in an era of striving. However, it is also an era of depravity! You see, most of those who serve in companies, firms, and other institutions are young people in their twenties. Take another look, and those who are lost in the world of sensual pleasures, dogs, and horses are also mostly young people in their twenties! I think that at this time, it is when you are spreading your branches and leaves. You should not let them run wild but restrain them. You will see that the lush trees will become withered branches. Isn't this too regrettable? I think that if you hold on to a fixed purpose and do not blindly follow others, then you can gradually reach a stable path. XX XX XX

Step by step, you will reach

The Crossroads of Death (8)

— Fan Yanqiao

3. Abandoning a Lagging One

Is it that revolution shouldn't forget love? Or that changing love shouldn't forget revolution? Or that both revolution and love are needed? The simple-minded Young Master Han Muliang has already forgotten. In short, since he arrived in the capital, he saw at Xuanwu Lake, by the Qinhuai River, on Qingliang Mountain, beside Yuhuatai, and all other places where one could climb and gaze, there was always a man and a woman, very intimately talking and laughing together, coming and going, sitting and standing. A woman with permed hair and dancing socks, leaning on the side of a man in military uniform with a soft leather whip, made him feel that the air of revolution was filled with love, and the tide of love stirred up revolution.

What made him even more unable to avoid jealousy, and from jealousy to hate, were the frequent banquets.

He remembered, on the eighth day of taking office at the XX Department, many colleagues held a welcome dinner at the Anle Restaurant. In one room, two tables were set, men and women mixed together, their laughter and the scent of perfume filling the air, harmonizing the dry flattery, fawning, enumeration, exaggeration, boasting, envy, and various different methods of (blowing) and (patting). Mrs. Feng, the section chief, speaking in crisp Beijing dialect about the old capital's miniature golf, was more pleasant to listen to than Mei Lanfang's opera. Mrs. Li, the section chief, liked to gamble and was most experienced with the Shanghai greyhound races, and her authentic Shanghai dialect was not annoying either. What attracted the most attention from the whole room was the dancing skills of Comrade Chang Shanfen, a clerk. Foxtrots, waltzes... she used her slender hand, adorned with a four-carat diamond ring, to simulate the steps on the edge of the round table instead of her jade feet in high heels, and even moved her head from side to side, lightly humming a marching tune in her mouth, so that even the stably placed artificial ivory chopsticks almost wanted to dance with her.

In the end, the men were plain and crude, only able to praise the greatness of "Secrets of the Imperial Palace," the poetic nature of Hu Die's two dimples, that the Western food at Mercier's was not as good as at the Lexiang Restaurant, that the Nanjing cheongsams were too short, and that Suzhou was too calm. These words almost made the tartar jump out of their ears. Don't listen to them, let's appreciate the women's faces and makeup instead. That one with a few strands of hair at the hairline is quite charming. That one's rouge on her lips is too thick, she doesn't even dare to eat much food. It's better to be like the one at that table, who only draws fine eyebrows, applies Paris dry powder, and doesn't (dot rouge on her lips), which is more generous and natural.

Page 13

The Anhui Provincial Association of All Anhui Tea Industries in Shanghai, the Xiuxihui Wuyuan Tea Industry Association, and all Tea Merchants jointly received an order from the Ministry instructing the Anhui Finance Department not to set up checkpoints along the river to collect original business tax, and to handle the case where Cao Yan and other tax guarantors in Xiuxihui did not comply with the Ministry's order and dispatched troops to set up checkpoints along the river to collect taxes and additionally levy tea tax. A telegram was sent appealing. The text of the telegram is recorded below: Respectfully addressed to the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, Supervisory Yuan, Hankou Military Affairs Committee, Chairman Chiang, and the Kuomintang and Political Affairs Supervisory Committee: We have carefully examined the Business Tax Law, which has already been promulgated and implemented. Article 4 stipulates that the business tax rate shall be levied at a rate of four to twenty per thousand of the business capital amount. Article 9 states that the business tax shall be paid directly by the taxpayer to the collection agency, and shall not be contracted or handled by others. The laws and decrees are brilliant, and financial authorities and business people should abide by them together. However, the Anhui Finance Department, in the spring of this year, under the name of special business, contracted the business tax of tea in She and Xiu counties to merchants Chen Changde, Shi Yuyu, Cao Zai, and Wang Xuehua. Chen Changde and others recognized the package rules of 28,080 yuan and set up checkpoints along the river at Huizhou, Tunxi, Shendu Street, and other places to collect taxes according to the original tea tax method. At that time, merchants knew that the matter was illegal, but they endured it silently because the tax rate had not increased. Unexpectedly, the tax contractors Chen Changde and others still harbored evil intentions, and they presented to the Anhui Finance Department and the Special Business Tax Bureau for approval to collect according to the tea capital tax rate of seventy per thousand in the 19th year, actually restoring the likin, and dispatched troops to coerce merchant Liu Shuzhi, who was forced to drown in the river and died. Merchants were sad and indignant, and unable to bear the oppression, they began to appeal to the Ministry and provinces. In mid-June, they received an order from the Ministry of Finance to levy taxes at a rate of five to twenty per thousand. Chen Changde and others then agreed to temporarily collect at a tax rate of twenty per thousand, and the remaining excessive amount was recorded in the account books using a registration method to temporarily avoid payment. From May to August of this year, until the date of suspension, in addition to the approximately 50,000 yuan that had been collected that did not exceed the tax rate of twenty per thousand, more than 10,000 yuan of illegal taxes had been collected, which was not a small amount. If the contractor Chen Changde and others can submit the legally collected tax amount, they will already have a surplus. However, the merchants concealed it and did not release it, and the Director of the Finance Department, Hua Yuanlong, for some unknown reason, did not pursue the tax contractors, but instead pursued the illegal taxes that the tea merchants had registered but not paid. He successively appointed special commissioners to guard and demand payment, ordering the She County Tea Industry Association to complete the payment on its behalf. Because this illegal tax amount had not been collected and there were no funds to pay, the tea merchants had no choice but to file an administrative appeal with the Anhui Provincial Government according to legal procedures. However, the provincial government delayed handling it, and the Finance Department did not wait for the provincial government's decision, nor did it stop the punishment. Committee member Zhang Siqing and others urged the She County Government to seal up the property of the chairman of the She County Tea Industry Association, threatening to auction it off to pay off the debt, acting swiftly and vigorously, as if dealing with bandits. It is truly unknown what crime the chairman of the tea merchants has committed, and that the official authorities should use force to such an extreme. If this tea likin of seventy per thousand is truly legal, then the merchants, even if they lose their homes and livelihoods, would not have the slightest complaint. Or if this money has already been deposited with the association, with most of the fellow merchants being nearby in the same village, how can the chairman of the tea merchants alone conceal it? Ye Yuanlong, the director of finance of a province, cannot pretend to be unaware of the National Government's order to abolish likin and the financial and criminal laws and regulations. He clearly knows that the abolition of likin concerns national credibility, but he brazenly levies a tea likin in disguise of seventy per thousand. He clearly knows that merchants have no obligation to pay illegal taxes, but he brazenly pursues them and seals up the property of innocent merchants. He shelters those who contract taxes for personal gain and exploit merchants, fearing that he is not doing enough, and he abuses law-abiding and tax-paying good merchants, fearing that he is not being cruel enough. The country still has laws and regulations, and the laws have not yet failed. What responsibility should Ye Yuanlong bear? The people of Huizhou have always been known for their simplicity and willingness to help others. Unless they are driven to the point of unbearable suffering, they would not dare to lightly trouble the authorities. We hereby truthfully state the facts, hoping that you will secretly send a high-ranking official to Anhui to thoroughly investigate and order the cessation of the illegal punishment of pursuing taxes and sealing property in order to maintain the rule of law and save the people's lives. We are filled with trepidation as we await your orders.
