Record of the Yishan Society Members' General Meeting

The Yishan Society of Shanghai was founded in the tenth year of the Republic by wealthy merchants such as Chen Yitang and Sun Jingpei. It has historically handled charitable and public welfare matters, such as providing medical care, medicine, rice, and poverty relief. Its expenses are generally borne by the members according to their abilities to donate. Yesterday, the eleventh general meeting was held to re-elect the board of directors, attended by over one hundred members. Zhang Shusheng was publicly elected as chairman. After the report, Zhang Yichen proposed to amend the constitution. After public deliberation, the amendments were passed item by item. Following the vote count, Zhang Qiaosheng, Ke Zhenwu, Chen Songyan, Yan Shiping, Wang Xingyuan, Ni Genghua, Liu Junliao, He Hanting, Chang Zhuoru, Zhang Yiqing, Ma Jintang, Ma Hanzhang, Zhou Zhuming, Ma Chunlin, and Liu Jifu, fifteen people were elected as directors, with Wang Desan, Zhang Yutang, Yu Yantang, Zhou Jinqin, and Zhuang Cuihu elected as alternate directors. Zhang Yichen was re-elected as chairman of the board, and Zhang Shusheng and Ma Jintang were elected as vice-chairmen.

French Concession Prohibits Entry into Residences for Property Seizure

The French Concession authorities, according to a statement by Fabre, the director-general of the French Municipal Police, have noted that certain mortgage loan companies, when borrowers fail to repay the loans in full on time, often enter the borrower's residences to seize the items mortgaged at the time of the loan. Such conduct, even if specified in the contract, is illegal. Hereafter, residents of the French Concession who encounter individuals acting in a private capacity, without the accompaniment of personnel from the Municipal Council or consular offices, entering residences and causing the aforementioned disputes, should immediately notify the police.

Fire in Kunming Road

The Minghua Silver Coin Manufacturing Factory at numbers 1-35 Kunming Road in Yangshupu caught fire at around five o'clock yesterday morning. Flames erupted, illuminating the sky. Twelve machines, over twenty boxes of manufactured silver mirrors, and several boxes of raw materials, as well as eight flat houses, were destroyed. The fire brigade arrived and made strenuous efforts to put out the fire, which was finally extinguished after seven o'clock. According to the investigation, the total loss is estimated at approximately 20,000 taels. It is reported that the factory had fire insurance.

Ju Jian's Bestselling

Mr. Huang Run wrote the book Ju Jian, based on his years of chrysanthemum cultivation experience, considering both new and old methods for cultivation, and adding illustrations that everyone can understand. Artists and growers have praised it highly. The different types of chrysanthemums have different cultivation methods that have changed from the past. Over the past few hundred years in Beijing, experts have researched propagation and breeding, making continuous progress. However, those who love the old despise the new, and those who like the new dislike the old. It is difficult to find someone who can integrate and thoroughly explain the reasons. The Lu Shi Yi Ju Zhi cites extensively, but omits details on cultivation methods. In modern times, with the development of science, soil and fertilizers are becoming more refined, with each flower able to reach a full diameter of more than a foot, which is rarely seen in ancient times. Mr. Huang has always loved growing chrysanthemums and has studied them deeply. His book, Ju Jian, gathers a wealth of theories and is truly a pioneering work in the horticultural world. Moreover, the price is very low (only one yuan), so it has been selling very well since publication. However, there are few books left, so those who love chrysanthemums should buy them quickly. The Shanghai Shen Bao also has consignment sales.

件費唐法官研究上海公共租界情形報告書第四卷（十六）

Chapter Four: Qualifications of Directors and Regulations on the Conduct and Tenure of Directors

1. (The provisions regarding the qualifications of directors as stated in the Land Regulations relate only to the economic qualifications of directors, that is, anyone who contributes a certain amount to the municipal revenue is qualified to be a director, as mentioned earlier, Note 1.) According to Clause 19 of the Land Regulations, the qualifications of directors are higher than those of voters. No one (unless, in addition to license fees, they pay a full fifty taels of land and house tax estimated by the Public Works Department each year, or the rent paid to the Public Works Department for their residence is estimated at one thousand one hundred taels each year) is eligible to be elected as a director.

2. Usually, municipal organization laws contain a clear provision that, under certain circumstances, one cannot be elected as a councilor or retain their position as a councilor. This type of disqualification generally includes the following:

(1) Anyone serving as an official of the Municipal Council or holding any lucrative position under the Municipal Council is not eligible to be elected as a councilor or serve as a councilor.

(2) Any director who, without leave of absence, fails to attend Municipal Council meetings for a certain period shall be immediately dismissed.

(3) Except in certain exceptional cases, if a director has an economic relationship with a contract made by the Municipal Council, the director shall immediately recuse themselves.

(4) Anyone who has committed a serious crime and has been convicted, declared mentally unsound by the competent court, or declared bankrupt and whose debts have not been cleared is not qualified to be elected as a director or retain their position as a director.

3. For the purpose of providing an example, the provisions of the Tianjin British Concession Land Regulations regarding the above (1), (3), and (4) are quoted as follows: Article 14 (1) Notwithstanding the provisions of Article 13, anyone in any of the following circumstances is not qualified to be elected as a director or to serve as a director:

(A) The Municipal Auditor, or anyone serving as an official or holding any lucrative position under the authority or disposal of the Board of Directors.

(B) Anyone who, either personally or through their partners, has a direct or indirect share or interest in any contract made with the Board of Directors or on behalf of the directors, or in any business undertaken by the directors.

(2) However, no one shall be disqualified from being elected as a director or serving as a director, or be deemed to have a share or interest in such a contract or undertaking, solely because they have a share or interest in the following matters:

(A) Any lease, sale, or purchase of land, or any contract for the lease, sale, or purchase of land.

(B) Any contract for borrowing money, or any guarantee solely for the payment of money.

(C) Contracts awarded through public bidding, in which the director concerned has not participated in the vote on whether or not to accept them.

(D) Any newspaper publishing any advertisements concerning municipal affairs, or,

(E) Any contract entered into by any limited liability company with the Board of Directors regarding the supply of electric light, water, or any other matter within the municipality. (3) Any director who is accused of committing an indictable offense or is subject to bankruptcy proceedings shall not continue to hold their position as a director.

4. Apart from any explicit provisions on this issue, I firmly believe that the various restrictions on the qualifications and conduct of directors mentioned above have, in the past, been largely considered reasonable and necessary by the enlightened society within the Public Concession and have therefore been observed by the parties concerned. However, in view of the proposals that have been put forward (Note 2), namely (i) to increase the number of directors and (ii) to extend the term of office of directors to two years, I believe that when the Land Regulations are amended, it is appropriate to include explicit provisions regarding this matter. I do not wish to elaborate on how this provision should be worded, but I can briefly discuss a few points.

5. Although the ineligibility of Public Works Department officials to serve as directors is not explicitly stipulated in the Land Regulations, I firmly believe that this restriction has been considered necessary in the past and that the current Public Works Department should not allow any official to stand as a candidate for director or allow the appointment of any director to any position under the control of the Board of Directors while also allowing them to retain their seat as a director. This can be safely assumed without any doubt. However, for the sake of future protection, it seems advisable to have a clear provision that if the distinction between directors and Public Works Department officials is not strictly maintained, and officials of all levels of the Public Works Department are deemed eligible to be elected as directors, then the nature of the Public Works Department and the entire governance of the Public Concession will soon be completely changed. However, as things stand, this change may be achieved without even changing the text of the Land Regulations.

It should be noted that foreign employees of the Public Works Department are exempt from paying house tax and other municipal taxes according to their service regulations, so they currently cannot obtain the qualifications necessary for voters or directors.

6. As for the vacancy of a director due to non-attendance at meetings, Clause 47 of the amended Board of Directors Rules contains the following provision:

For the welfare of society, it is hereby proposed that any director who needs to leave Shanghai for three months or more should submit their resignation to the Chairman for their disposal so that when the Board of Directors decides to elect a replacement to fill the vacancy, they may proceed with the election. According to Article 20 of the Land Regulations, vacancies for current directors (if there are no more than three vacancies, may be filled by the serving directors through a plurality vote).

If the term of office of directors is extended from one year to two years, it is clearly even more important to establish a regulation regarding vacancies for directors due to frequent non-attendance at meetings or due to inability to attend meetings due to leaving Shanghai, illness, or other reasons.

7. The nature of the regulation regarding the economic relationship between directors and contracts made by the Public Works Department is one of the most difficult issues that has been discussed. However, this issue is particularly important because, after the number of directors is increased in the future, it will affect the high degree of financial integrity that the Public Works Department has the ability to maintain, which has been a characteristic of its administration.

8. The Public Works Department's rules of procedure contain the following provisions to restrict the right of directors of the Board of Directors and members of committees to speak or vote on matters with which they have an economic relationship:

(Article 34: Any director who has an economic relationship with a matter scheduled for discussion shall declare such relationship, and shall comply if requested by the Chairman not to speak, vote, or withdraw from the meeting.)

(Article 77: Any member who has an economic relationship with a matter scheduled for discussion shall declare such relationship, and shall comply if requested by the other members not to speak, vote, or withdraw from the meeting.)

9. Although the above two rules are based on the principle that a director or member should not vote or try to influence their colleagues' votes on any matter if they have a private economic relationship with that matter, the procedure of this provision is open to criticism. This is because it does not unconditionally prohibit the speech or vote of the director or member concerned, but leaves the question of whether or not to prohibit it to the discretion of the Chairman in one case and to the members of the committee concerned in the other. This may sometimes cause embarrassment or resentment to the Chairman or the committee's decision. I believe that a more appropriate approach would be to establish a definite standard whereby a director or member may not participate in the discussion or vote on any matter with which they have an economic relationship, or may even be required to withdraw from the meeting room when the matter is brought up for debate or put to a vote. However, an exception may be made if the relationship of the director or member is shared by the majority of the public. Another point to note is that the existing wording seems to refer only to the personal economic relationship of the director or committee member, and does not explicitly include the economic relationship of the firm or company that employs the director or member.

In an appendix to this report (Note 3), I have cited the more definitive and comprehensive provisions of the Durban Transvaal Municipal Regulations regarding this issue as an illustration.

10. In addition to the issue of restricting directors or members from speaking or voting on any matter with which they have an economic relationship, there is also the issue of whether directors or members should have any relationship with any contract made by the Public Works Department, with certain limited exceptions. When considering this issue, one must take into account, on the one hand, the need to effectively protect the public interest so that directors or members do not seek to use their position to advance their private interests, and on the other hand, the need to avoid establishing unnecessary restrictions that would deter responsible businessmen from serving as directors because such restrictions would harm their personal business or the business of the firm or company they represent. Strict restrictions may disqualify businessmen who are otherwise qualified to be directors, which would risk weakening the talent of the Board of Directors. Moreover, if contracts made by the municipality with which the director or the firm they represent have an economic relationship can be guaranteed to be public, there would not be a serious risk of directors improperly using their position. This has already been acknowledged elsewhere.

11. From this perspective, there are only two options for adoption: (1) to prohibit directors from entering into contracts with the Public Works Department or having a relationship with contracts made by the Public Works Department, with certain limited exceptions; (2) to establish a regulation that (A) any relationship between a contract made with the Public Works Department and a director shall be formally disclosed so that it is known to all; (B) the director concerned shall not participate in the discussion or vote on issues relating to the contract.

In an appendix to this report (Note 4), I have cited provisions of the Durban Transvaal Municipal Regulations that serve as an illustration of two alternative approaches to this issue.

(Note 1) See Section 30 of Chapter Six of Part Five of this report.

(Note 2) See the reform plans (3) and (6) in Chapter Six (Section E) of Part Five of this report.

(Note 3) See Appendix 43, Article 41 of the Local Government Ordinance of 1926.

(Note 4) See Appendix 43, Articles 39 and 40 of the Local Government Ordinance of 1926, and see Articles 38 and 42 of the same ordinance, which prohibit municipal councilors from competing for any specialized professional awards, whether in support of family associations or in opposition to the municipal council, and do not allow municipal councilors to attend, as parties concerned, the valuation tribunals established by the municipal council or the licensing committees organized by the municipal council. (To be continued)

Supplement of Shen Bao Local News

Commentary

Sutra Chanting, Temple Building, and Education

— Tian Fang

Recently, things in society seem a bit "abnormal," perhaps what biologists call "recessive reappearance" or what psychologists call "atavism"? Otherwise, why do we feel like we are treading in the footsteps of the past everywhere we go?

If you don't believe me, look at the sutra chanting in Beiping. Now, immortals are no longer born into the world, but there are still Buddhist masters in Shanghai, which can be considered fortunate. According to reports, the Vajra Dharma Assembly received a total of three to five hundred thousand donations from various parties, spending no less than two or three hundred thousand gold, how grand! It would make the little monks speechless. It's comparable to Emperor Wu of Liang in recent times, and traces back to the era of the Investiture of the Gods, which is probably not too far off. It's a pity that they couldn't curse the wooden clogs to death, which is a great regret. It's probably because the other side also has deities. When deities meet, it's like positive and negative forces opposing each other in physics, and the effects cancel each other out. The merits of the recent Dharma Assembly have just been completed, and the construction of a temple is about to begin. A Nanjing telegram reported the other day that thirty thousand was needed to repair the Confucius Temple, and the National Government is urging the Ministry of Finance to allocate the funds, which shows that the country cares for both military strength and cultural advancement. It truly takes both sides into account. Only the Ministry of Finance has a title but no money, and the common people have lives but no wealth. The educational expenses of Pingjin have been owed for a long time, and the teachers of Lanzhou Elementary School have gone on strike due to a lack of funds. (See Xi'an telegram on the 2nd of this month as reported). How fortunate to be dead? How unfortunate to be alive?

Since the Confucius Temple is related to ancient Chinese culture and its architecture is worth preserving, although I am not a disciple of the sage, I do not have any objections. However, this is something that should be done when the country is at peace and the national treasury is abundant, not at the present time. Confucius once criticized Guan Zhong for his "three returns" and the Lu for "carving rafters." Now, he cannot escape this either? Reciting the words "If you cannot serve people, how can you serve ghosts?" I can't help but sigh three times.

Or it is said that building temples and chanting sutras is not for the dead, but for the living. In that case, I have no objections.

Science

Common Misunderstandings About Biology (Continued)

— Xiaoguang

(6) Bats are Transformed from Mice

Bats and mice have somewhat similar head shapes, and both reside in secluded places of people's homes, venturing out at night to find food. Therefore, some people say that bats are transformed from mice. This is a (similar inference) error. In zoology, bats belong to the order Chiroptera of mammals (not birds), while mice belong to the order Rodentia. Bats have thin membranes stretched between their limbs and tail, allowing them to fly, and they feed on insects. Their habits are completely different from those of mice.

(7) Crabs Have No Blood

In some local dialects, the phrase "(no)" is often replaced by "(crab blood)". However, it's just not red. Its heart is composed of a single atrium and a single ventricle, serving circulatory functions. It breathes through gills, taking in oxygen from the water to purify the blood. Also, Bao Puzi says: "(In the mountains, what is called the 'Intestineless Gentleman' is the crab)"; the common saying that crabs have "(seven legs, eight hands, and no intestines)" is also a misunderstanding.

(8) Rhinoceros Horns Can Illuminate Demons and Divide Water

The legend that rhinoceros horns can illuminate demons probably originated from the Book of Jin: "When Wen Qiao arrived at Niuzhu Islet, the water was too deep to measure, and the world said that there were many monsters underneath. Qiao then burned a rhinoceros horn and illuminated it. After a short while, he saw aquatic creatures covering the fire, strange and bizarre shapes." This is unfounded. Rhinoceros are a type of herbivorous animal, slightly smaller than elephants, with hairless, extremely thick skin. In ancient times, it was used to make armor. Those produced in Tibet and India have one horn on their nose, called the one-horned rhinoceros; those produced in Africa have two horns on their nose, called the two-horned rhinoceros. The horn is dense and hard, and can be used to make utensils or for medicinal purposes. Both of these types of rhinoceros like to swim, with their horns exposed above the water, advancing across the waves. Therefore, those who see them mistakenly believe that rhinoceros horns can divide water.

(9) Ghost Howling

The belief that humans have souls after death is almost a universal concept among various peoples of the world. It is said that souls have perception and can act, and of course they can also speak. Thus, the superstition of "ghost howling" has been fabricated! Li Hua's Elegy for the Ancient Battlefield says: "Often overturning entire armies, often with ghosts crying, heard on cloudy days." Du Fu's Ballad of the Army Carts says: "New ghosts are troubled by injustice, old ghosts cry, with the sound of chirping on cloudy and rainy days." They speak so decisively, as if it were true. However, the origin of sound lies in the vibration of objects. When a person dies, the body decomposes and the spiritual function also disappears with it. Where would there be a soul? Where would there be ghost howling? Wang Chong's Lun Heng: "Whenever there are ghosts between heaven and earth, they are not made by the spirits of the dead, but are all caused by people's thoughts and imaginations. How is this caused? It is due to illness. When people are sick, they worry and fear, and worry and fear are where ghosts come from." This is very true—the so-called ghost howling is actually the cry of a night bird (commonly known as the owl). Suiyuan Shihua records Wang Fengting's poem: "Strange bird's voice is like a ghost, and dark tree shadows resemble people." This can be said to be exactly what I think.

(10) Cucumbers and Peanuts Cannot Be Eaten Together

Cucumbers (Hu gua) are commonly known as yellow melons or cucumbers. Zhang Qian brought their seeds from the Western Regions during his mission, hence the name. Peanuts are also known as "longevity fruits." They bloom in late summer and autumn, with yellow, butterfly-shaped flowers. After the flowers, the ovary enters the ground, forming pods, hence the name "falling peanuts." It is said that these two fruits cannot be eaten together, and that eating them together is enough to harm life. Some people have analyzed their ingredients, and no trace of toxic substances can be detected, no matter how they are combined. Furthermore, eating them together for a long time has no adverse effects.

Loyal Sails Swallowed by This

Society Improvement Discussion Group

Reply to the Criticism of "Abolishing the Evil Custom of Teasing the Newlyweds"

— Xiaoxue

"Humans are emotional and excitable animals, at least partially true, because of this…the rituals and red tape of the human world become excessive." Wen Bingjun starts by expounding the elements of social evolution. However, social evolution and human civilization require rational consideration in addition to emotion. Indeed, actions based on emotion and momentary excitement are often wrong. Only reason can judge the good and evil of things. If an act of exciting emotion is not rationally considered, it can be called evil because it hinders social evolution. Then, a custom that is carried down through tradition without rational thought can be called an evil habit. Therefore, teasing the newlyweds is no exception.

The initiator of teasing the newlyweds (a speculation, as it cannot be verified) may have given it consideration, but gradually, under tradition, to the present, the consideration has long been buried and forgotten. That is why there are barbaric acts because of a lack of consideration. If you ask someone who has just finished teasing the newlyweds: "Old X, why are you teasing the newlyweds?" He will definitely stare blankly, or say: "Teasing the newlyweds is to have fun. Drinking alone is boring, don't you understand?" This phenomenon is prevalent in the psychology of the masses, even among the intelligentsia.

It is precisely because the true meaning of teasing the newlyweds has been lost, it is precisely because modern people lack rational consideration, and it is precisely because it relies on emotional action and the action of excitement that I have proposed its abolition.

The above paragraphs of theory can prove that it is an evil habit of society. And Mr. Wen's saying that I am "deliberately making dangerous words" is a bit too arbitrary and without consideration?! Mr. Wen's examples of A, B, and C are "feared" to be fictional, which needs to be corrected. When I wrote this article, I tried my best to shorten the length. Therefore, the statement of facts was too simple, which made Mr. Wen suspect that it was "feared" to be fictional. This fact was obtained from my exploration among married and unmarried young students. Their psychology is all like this, and it has also taken shape in facts. Mr. Wen has not seen it, but I have explored it and seen it.

Mr. Wen believes that the conflict between the groom and the guests is "perhaps" (accidental). If Mr. Wen looks around and looks at the whole of China, he will know that it is not "perhaps" "accidental"! But it often happens!

If Mr. Wen does not "fear" that teasing the newlyweds is an evil habit, please refer to the Jiangxi tricks in the News Tea Talk column, a little bit about the tricks in Shanghai and its surroundings, and a little bit about the tricks in the whole Chinese society!

Mr. Wen sits in Shanghai and shouts "advocate", but it only increases the sins of Chinese society!

Evil Customs

The October Morning Festival

— Shiben

The "tang, tang, tang" of the gong powerfully pierced my eardrums. Then there was a burst of noise and a cacophony of musical instruments, coming from far away, melodious and moving. Ah! Which family is welcoming a new bride again? I wondered in my heart.

Stepping out of the door, it was dark and crowded. Many people from the neighborhood had already gathered, men and women dressed in colorful clothes, flocking from all directions. Today's excitement had already violently broken through the quiet atmosphere of Town A, which was so calm that you could catch ghosts.

After a burst of hubbub and deafening music, I saw triangular flags with red silk and green edges, embroidered with golden dragons with claws, fluttering and dancing, coming in a mighty and grand procession. Behind them followed pairs of signboards with white characters on black backgrounds and gold characters on red backgrounds, and the luanjia of swords, spears, and all kinds of weapons. These things filled with feudal colors, obsolete and outdated objects, passed by like shuttles in a never-ending stream. Ah! I guessed wrong, it's not someone's wedding, but some kind of play of welcoming gods and holding a festival. So I couldn't help but sigh deeply. Alas! Internal troubles and external invasions, the country is about to perish. The proper and urgent national salvation movement is not being done, but people are excitedly and enthusiastically doing this kind of ignorant, wasteful, and prohibited act of welcoming gods and holding festivals. It is truly a drunken dream. But I was not touched by the scenery and felt sad and sighed. Instead, the crowd was filled with an atmosphere of approval and welcome. Burning incense, lighting candles, worshipping, everyone was smiling happily and enthusiastically rejoicing. The people in the shops on both sides also cracked their mouths, pointing east and west, enthusiastically talking:

"Hee hee, the Tiangang flag is coming! I remember that there are thirty-six Tiangang flags in total. The first one is the Liangshan hero, Song Gongming, who assassinated Yan Poxi!"

"Lao Sun, look, the two signboards 'Xiao Jing' (Silence) and 'Tao Dun' (Escape) are here!" The young clerk in the southern goods store said to a colleague named Sun.

"Hum! Shameless, you should know the commander-in-chief of the Bai Liao. These two signboards, one is called 'Su Jing' (Quiet) and the other is called 'Hui Bi' (Avoidance). You read them as 'Xiao Jing Tao Dun.' It seems that your characters were taught by Confucius's great-grandmother!" The clerk surnamed Sun said, proudly, and the young clerk next to him was ashamed and red-faced.

"Look, look, the imperial mandate is here! Oh dear, this old man is really imposing. There are eight imperial mandates! No wonder he is so efficacious! Ordinary goblins and monsters will immediately shiver when they see his eight imperial mandates, so when people get sick and ask for this old man, they will get better immediately, because he has many imperial mandates." These feudal, nonsensical, superstitious words were spoken by a man who looked like a merchant.

"Oh! It's so beautiful! There are also people carrying incense pillars participating! Hahahaha…" Amid the applause and shouts of joy, more than a dozen courageous, spirited, and energetic young villagers appeared, all with bare arms, and many iron hooks pierced into their arms, tied with a red rope, with stone lions, flower pots, and other things hanging below. This is called "carrying incense pillars". Alas! Courageous, piercing good meat with iron hooks and hanging thirty or forty pounds of things, it's a pity that this kind of self-sacrificing spirit is not used to serve the country, but is used for this superstitious act. "The old man is here! Quickly light firecrackers to welcome him!" With a burst of loud firecrackers, I saw many people crowding around a wooden puppet, coming. The shop owners across the street respectfully knelt down and kowtowed like pounding garlic, and they all burned incense and burned silver ingots, busying themselves happily.

The sound of the gong rang, and a group of ignorant men and women, again crowded the wooden puppet to another place. After watching, I went inside, and my mother asked me, "Shi'er, was the October Morning Festival good to watch today?"

Joke

Umbrellas and Chamber Pots

— Ying Shi

In our village, there was a gentleman who was very wealthy. People flattered him by calling him a local tycoon. However, he had never attended school. Whenever people borrowed money or items from him, he would always draw pictures in his account book to keep track. For example, if he lent several dozen silver dollars, he would draw several dozen circles representing silver dollars. If he lent several bowls, he would draw several bowl shapes.

He had a relative through marriage who was an unsuccessful scholar. His family was quite poor. Once, he came to visit when the tycoon was out, so he sat alone in silence. Suddenly, he saw the account book on the table and aimlessly flipped through it. "Oh my," he thought, "how can such a good account book be made so dirty and unsightly?" So he asked the family's servant, "What is this used for?" The servant replied, "That is my master's account book. All the silver money lent out and goods bought in are written in this account book." Upon hearing this, the scholar sighed deeply. "Alas," he said, "how can such an illiterate man become rich, while I, though untalented, am still a scholar, be so impoverished?" He sighed with emotion and wrote the words "fate" on the account book with his brush, then left.

Later, the illiterate tycoon returned and saw the marks on the account book. He asked the servant, "Was there anyone here while I was out?" The servant replied, "It was so-and-so, your relative by marriage, who came to visit." When he heard this, he threw the account book on the table and said angrily, "I told you not to associate with these poor devils. They come running here just to borrow an umbrella and find a chamber pot!" Haha, he thought the character "fate" was a drawing of an umbrella, and the character "also" was a drawing of a chamber pot. The shapes were somewhat similar, which was truly laughable.

A Corner of Society

Prepared but Not Used

— Zu Lai

Mr. Wang, the accountant, suggested, "The world is going downhill, and thieves are active day and night. We are truly in danger with silver dollars coming in and out all day long. Therefore, I suggest we install an alarm bell, prepared but not used. What do you all think?" The colleagues agreed unanimously with Mr. Wang and praised him for his thoroughness.

Three days later, a square red glass lantern was found above the main gate of XX business. The words "Alarm" were written on the glass.

Unexpectedly, by sheer coincidence, robbers came to the door less than a week later. One guarded the main gate, one guarded the back gate, and four others rushed into the counter with pistols. "Be sensible!" one of the robbers said fiercely.

The colleagues, seeing the four pistols, were so frightened that their souls flew out of their bodies. Some crawled under the stools, and others hid under the counter. They had long forgotten about the alarm bell. The robbers unceremoniously took the three thousand yuan in banknotes and four hundred yuan in cash from the table and swaggered away.

The colleagues, seeing that the robbers had left, slowly crawled out from under the stools or the counter, but their faces were pale and they were as stiff as wooden chickens. After a long time, they began to argue. "Why didn't you press the alarm bell?" "If I pressed the alarm bell, would you want to keep your life?" "When I saw the pistol, my soul was gone. How could I think of pressing the alarm bell?" "Ah, life is dangerous!" Mr. Li, known as the king of humor, interjected, "This is what you call 'prepared but not used'!"

Nonsense

In the Courtroom

— Kang Shi

(1)

Judge: Why did you rob people?

Thug: Because I was hungry and had no food, and cold and had no clothes, so I became a robber and robbed people.

Judge: If you have no clothes and no food, you should find a job. How can you rob people?

Thug: In this time of economic decline, the number of unemployed is increasing every day. Where can you find a job? And to start a small business, the registration fee is not enough to cover the expenses. If you don't pay the registration fee, you have to use small copper coins to pay respects to the XX gentlemen and suffer a lot of injustice. Alas! Alas! Those who have not experienced it themselves will never know the suffering of society!

Judge: Now, according to Article XX of the law, I sentence you to X years and X months of imprisonment. Do you accept it?

Thug: I accept it very much. I can no longer worry about being cold and hungry! The thug walked away with a smile on his face, as if he was very proud.

(2)

Judge: Why was the car driving so fast? It killed a pedestrian!

Big shot: Because driving fast shows off my status. If I didn't drive fast, why would I be driving a car?

Judge: I sentence you to pay the family of the deceased three hundred yuan in compensation. Does the car owner agree?

Big shot: What is three hundred yuan? My monthly expenses are more than three hundred yuan!

(3)

Plaintiff (female): The defendant started with affection but abandoned me in the end. Now he has a new lover and has discarded me like old shoes. Therefore, I am filing for divorce and demanding that the defendant pay 25,000 yuan in alimony because the defendant's assets are more than 100,000 yuan.

Judge: Defendant, the plaintiff is demanding 25,000 yuan in alimony. Are you willing to pay?

Defendant (male): I am not willing. I am only willing to pay 5,000 yuan.

Judge: Plaintiff, 5,000 yuan is enough. If the defendant has no money, there is nothing you can do. You can't skin him alive, can you?

Plaintiff (female): Oh...

Short Story

Night Raid

— Shan

An Imaginary Painting of the Righteous Army Recapturing Fanyang City: The great wheel of time has already brought us into the realm of autumn. This night was a cool, pleasant, and beautiful autumn night. A street in the west of the city was quiet. The pedestrians had already closed their doors and hid in their houses, waiting and praying for a peaceful tomorrow. Only the old trees along the street stood tall, bathed in the bleak electric light and the light breeze and drizzle. Their branches and leaves swayed, sending out rustling sounds. In the distance, the barking of dogs in the small alleys occasionally broke the silence of the night.

Suddenly, a dark, blurred figure, holding something like a pole in his hand, crawled forward like a snake from the end of the street, feeling his way with his hands and feet, sometimes hidden, sometimes visible. He crawled behind an old tree and hid himself. After a while, another shadow emerged in the same way. Then another. And another! In an instant, behind every old tree, there was a majestic shadow holding a pole and swaying.

It was midnight. The light rain gradually became heavy and violent. The wind howled and roared with all its might! Only the electric light still maintained its bleakness and gloom...

"Boom!" A sound like the collapse of heaven and earth came from outside the city gate. Five hundred righteous soldiers shouted in unison, pointing their guns at the city gate and rushing forward! The torches were held high, dyeing half the sky red. The shadows behind the old trees all jumped out into the center of the street, pulled out torches, and simultaneously moved the mechanisms on the poles. "Peng! Peng! Peng!" One person first rushed onto the city wall and chopped down the enemy soldier guarding it. He quickly opened the city gate, and five hundred tiger-like warriors surged in like a tide!

The enemies were having sweet dreams. They were awakened and hurriedly issued an emergency assembly order. Some of the enemies began to mobilize.

"Kill! Kill!" "Peng!" "Boom!" The curtain of terror was clearly drawn open! Reflected in people's eyes were torches! Blood! Heads! Corpses!

"Kill! Kill! Sons of China! The time has come! Settle the blood debt with the enemy tonight! Don't let a single one go! Drown the enemy in the blood of our Chinese nation! Kill! Kill!"

The enemy's line was shattered! The iron cavalry of the righteous army filled the four sides of the city!

Market News

Mr. Gu Zhaokui, a Doctor of Traditional Chinese Medicine: Mr. Gu Zhaokui, a doctor of traditional Chinese medicine, once served as a doctor in hospitals in Taizhou, China, etc. He is now employed by the Guanshengyuan Company as a full-time doctor. He has rich experience and has cured many serious illnesses. For example, the wife of Manager Xi of Guanshengyuan suffered from body temperature, and the wife of Director Fei of the Wujiang County Public Security Bureau suffered from fever and noma. Both were cured by Dr. Gu. Recently, it was heard that Dr. Gu and his wife, Ms. Xie Feiyu, a female doctor, have jointly compiled a book of simple and effective self-treatment methods for common family illnesses. The book is divided into five major sections: external diseases, internal injuries, gynecology, pediatrics, and surgery. All are based on years of experience and proven prescriptions, so that patients can use it to treat their illnesses themselves, and doctors can read it to help others. It is expected to be published next month. Dr. Gu resides at No. 5 Humu Villa, Liuxing Alley, west of Chuanxin River Bridge, Zhaojia Road, inside the Old West Gate.

Mu'er Hall National Defense Corps Seeks Members: The Youth Section of the Mu'er Hall on Xizang Road is affiliated with the National Defense Corps. Its purpose is pure, to promote morality, exercise the body, and serve the community. It is now seeking new members in this city. Any youth who aspire to good health can join. Bylaws will be sent upon request.

Shen Bao This City Supplement Movie Special

Republic of China Twenty-first Year, Eleventh Month, Eighth Day, Tuesday (No Separate Fee)

Overseas Rare News

Hollywood's Economic Recovery (Jieke)

The global economic panic has also severely hit Hollywood. Hollywood has 14,000 extras. They have been unemployed and starving for two years. Now, because Cecil B. DeMille is creating a great new historical film, "The Sign of the Cross," one-third of them have been able to eat milk and sandwiches again. Today's Hollywood is vibrant again, just like in the golden age. Every day at 5:30 p.m., hundreds and thousands of male and female actors in Roman costumes are collecting their salaries at the window of the Hollywood accounting office. On the sidewalks, there are ancient Christian believers, slaves in leopard skins, and men and women in Roman costumes mingling with the crowds. DeMille's genius has solved Hollywood's unemployment problem.

In January of this year, as soon as the news that DeMille was going to direct the new film "The Sign of the Cross" came out, he was immediately surrounded by actors. DeMille had to spend eighteen hours a day listening to the endless ringing of the phone and reading the snowflakes of letters. In front of his office, densely packed men and women shouted, "Mr. DeMille, for God's sake, use me! I haven't had anything to do for months. My wife relies on the relief association. My son is also sick. Have pity on me."

"This is so heartbreaking," DeMille said with a smile. "Wherever I go, they follow. Choosing a few and rejecting a few is really a heartbreaking job. For one scene, we have to choose fifty people from more than two hundred people. Looking at the faces of those who are rejected, ah, how uncomfortable it is."

DeMille's new film employs actors of all sizes, some for only a few days, some for the entire film. One scene features a group of Christians secretly praying by a grave on the edge of Rome. Roman soldiers shoot arrows one after another, killing many. Many actors pleaded mournfully not to be made to look like they were shot dead because once they were shot dead, they could no longer be used in the film.

Hollywood has 14,000 registered actors. Two years ago, most of them could make a living from filming. In the past, every film had to have a lively scene, otherwise the audience would not be satisfied. DeMille used 3,000 people in one scene in the film "The Ten Commandments." The filming of films such as "Ben-Hur" brought together hundreds of actors, married and had children, and gave them warmth and food for several years. Now, a scene with 200 people is considered very lively. After the success of DeMille's new film, it can recover a lot of the decline.

Coming Attractions

Another New Film by a Star Will Be Released Soon (Xiaogu)

Because Star Film Company wants to increase production, it has been working hard to recruit directors and actors in the past few months, preparing to open several more groups for filming. In addition to Hu Ping, Sun Min, Ai Xia, and Xuan Jinglin and Wang Ying, who are currently in negotiations, the director is Li Pingqian. Mr. Li has been with Tianyi Company for many years. The first film he directed was "Old Hatred and New Sorrow," written by Wang Qianbai. This is a story of pain caused by love. The plot is very intricate and stars Gong Jianong and Ai Xia. It is currently being directed by Mr. Li and working hard. It will be completed soon and is expected to be released in the middle of this month.

Anecdotes of Movie Stars

The Original Appearance of Stars (Sipei)

The comedian Charlie Chaplin always wears a mustache, old clothes, and a pair of broken leather shoes when he acts in movies. However, his original appearance is very handsome. It is only because of years of hard work, coupled with the divorce, that he is in a bad mood, and his hair has turned gray.

A Movie That Can Be Smelled (Jieke)

The saying that science is omnipotent is a proven fact that does not need to be proven again today. The movie thing has created an amazing record in recent years due to the progress of science. In the past, silent and colorless films have now become sound and color films, which are popular all over the world. People's joys, sorrows, anger, curses, words, songs, cries, and even the collapse of mountains and seas and the roars of lions and tigers in the universe, all sounds can now be easily heard in the films. Now comes a peculiar news saying that European and American scientists will soon invent a movie that can be smelled. If we believe that science is omnipotent, then this news is reliable. The source of this news is this. The British Science Association held a meeting in London in September this year. A scientist declared that he firmly believed that smelly movies would soon become a reality. We will soon be able to smell the fragrance of flowers on the film. In the past, Hollywood needed to select shadows and dubbing, but in the future, it will select odors.

Marie Dressler is a very beautiful and fair-skinned girl on the screen, but her original appearance is covered with freckles.

Douglas Fairbanks's face is very dark and full of beards. If he doesn't shave for a day or two, and kisses his wife Mary Pickford, the stiff whiskers will touch her tender cheeks, and a good wife may even cry out in pain.

John Gilbert is a famous young man in the film industry. He is very handsome, but his big nose and long neck are famous in Hollywood. If the collar of his costume is not properly made, or the photographer does not pay attention to the angle of photography, then the shortcomings of his long neck and big nose will be easily exposed to the audience.

Tom Mix, a star of horsemanship, still plays the role of a Western cowboy in love with young girls. He is nearly fifty years old, and deep wrinkles have grown on his forehead. Fortunately, there is a makeup box to repair and cover up, so he looks only thirty years old.

William Powell often plays the role of gangsters and thugs, but he is a noble gentleman himself. People in Hollywood call him "Uncle William," which shows his kindness and amiability.

The deceased movie star Lon Chaney was known for disguising himself as disabled freaks and performing venomous and cruel personalities. However, he himself was physically strong and very kind by nature. Even the doorman of the MGM film company where he served, he condescended to be friendly with, and there was no arrogance at all. Therefore, when the bad news came that Lon Chaney had died, many people were heartbroken for him.

Opinions and Contributions

A Brief Review of Domestic Films (Lu Meng)

Movies in modern times can be said to be at their peak! Of course, the development of this industry is not only due to the welcome of the people in society, but its existence in terms of value really occupies a very important component. In recent years, domestic films have sprung up like mushrooms after rain, adding a lot of light to the future of Chinese films. I will write about my humble opinion.

On the Trends of Soviet Films in the Past Fifteen Years (Continued) (Shi Yi)

(According to the opinions of Harry Alan Potamkin)

In the study of the progress of Soviet films, we may as well talk about the personal experiences of its film artists. As far as Protozanov is concerned, he directed "Aelita" and "The Man from the Restaurant." One of these films was the worst film influenced by Germany. This influence belonged to an incorrect type of proletariat; but after that, he also produced several of the best comedies, depicting in detail the aggressive "St. George's Holiday" and "Siberian Sentinels." Protozanov is one of the ancestors of Soviet films; he proposed the theory of Montage very early. Although he is still unwilling to forget the traces of his early past, he is able to give his films a lively vitality with his unique talent for "humor," which is where he is good at dealing with himself.

We cannot but admire the spirit and efforts of those engaged in the film industry, but there are still many shortcomings, so we believe that it is necessary to discuss them.

Error in Concept: At present, the general film industry often uses "sensuality" and "glamour" to please the lustful audience and seek to satisfy its box office. This low-level mentality is really enough to make the film itself bankrupt. I do not admit that this is driven by the social environment, but an error in concept. They have forgotten the true meaning of film art, which is to suggest the transformation of behavior, so that the films produced are all regarded as "entertainment" and "toys," brandishing weapons, which cannot but make people sigh!

Naivety of Consciousness: This is probably something that no one can deny. Of course, modern European and American films are not worthy of saying that their consciousness is very noble and rich, but they are much better than China. Originally, "consciousness" is the most important thing in the film. If the "consciousness" is not strong, there will be no impression on the audience, and there is even the danger of being worthless. The problem with Chinese films in the past twenty years is that they only know "imitation" and do not know "creation," so "consciousness" has also been greatly affected. Then its naivety is of course also in the absolute possibility. We only need to watch domestic films a few more times to discover this situation.

Director's Imperfection: In the filming process, the most important responsibility is the director. He is the person who translates a readable script into a visible action. Since his task is so important, then his difficulties of course also arise. Therefore, a director must not only have sufficient various ideas, but also have a long time of preparation; but Chinese film directors mostly act hastily, so that after the entire production is completed, "flaws" emerge in clusters, and the plot in the film often has "incomplete" and "flaws," which easily loses the integrity and spirit of action expression.

The above are all obvious points. There are many other trivial matters. Because of the limited space, I cannot make a detailed discussion. I will stop my clumsy writing here. I hope that the Chinese film industry will pay more attention! Twenty-first, eleventh, one, in Jiangwan

Local News

A Car Dispute (Mai)

In general, celebrities are used to riding in their own cars. Once they lose them, they still need that extravagant material enjoyment in their hearts. So what happens when they don't have them? Naturally, they have to hire a taxi. I remember around the end of last month, the big star Zhang Zhiyun rented a car number 18306 from Liyi Taxi Company. She rented it for four consecutive days. On the fifth day (that is, the third of this month), Huang, the Liyi driver, received news of Zhiyun's move, so he drove the car to find her to ask for money. The driver's knowledge was too shallow. He didn't understand the art of collecting debts, and his words inevitably offended Ms. Zhang, so she called two young men in suits and a young lady, and they started a fight in the alley! Who knew that these weak young men in suits were not good at fighting. The driver knocked them into the gutter with three punches and two kicks, getting them covered in sewage. The driver took the opportunity to run to the Shanzhong Road police station to report. The police station immediately sent Detective Zhou, along with the driver, to Ms. Zhang's residence to ask about the situation. The driver said, "Ms. Zhang rented the car for four days and didn't pay a penny, and she kept delaying. She even stopped riding in Liyi's cars and started riding in Yunfei's cars, and she even gathered a crowd to use violence!" Ms. Zhang blamed the driver for being barbaric! Rude! And she lost two diamonds and a watch. The detective asked her, "Since you lost valuable jewelry, of course you have to report it and sue." Ms. Zhang said very generously and frankly, "Diamonds are nothing, a small matter, no need to sue." Since the principal does not care about suing, but returning to the main topic, it is still necessary to collect the debt. Ms. Zhang agreed to have them come to collect it at ten o'clock that night.

At ten o'clock that night, Detective Zhou and Liyi's accountant went to collect the payment. The total amount was 81 yuan and 50 cents. Ms. Zhang gave a discount and paid 64 yuan and 50 cents, thus clearing the matter.

Don't Need Relatives (Ming)

Many Hollywood stars often provide their relatives with money or find them jobs, but they always send those relatives to places far away from Hollywood. The farther away, the happier the stars are, because they believe that having relatives is good, but they don't want relatives swarming around them.

Garbo Was Suddenly Discovered! (Ai)

Because so many people want to know Greta Garbo's personality and actions, the New York Times sent a special reporter to Europe to find her. Unexpectedly, on the third day of the reporter's ship, a very seductive classical girl was suddenly discovered. She was only wearing shorts and a shirt, slowly strolling on the deck. This was Garbo, who had been searched for everywhere. The whole ship was surprised and stunned! It is strange that Garbo would be so unrestrained.

Film Monograph

The Emperor Receives His Mandate from Heaven (Chen Dabei)

Confucius said, "To know it is not as good as to love it; to love it is not as good as to delight in it." If we want a unique and correct path in Chinese films, we cannot but hope that there will be more loyal comrades who love and delight in the art of performance. Because the art of performance cannot be learned by reading a few articles of lofty discussions. Therefore, it is not enough to just seek knowledge. One must love and delight in it, learn and practice it constantly, in order to succeed.

"Can screen stars really be made by themselves?" Such a question is often asked in both the United States and China. What is the value of this question?

May I ask, if screen stars are not made by themselves, can it be said that they are made by others? Can it be said that they must be made by heaven?

That's right. Many people do believe that stars are made by heaven. Such people not only think this way about screen stars, but they also think this way about all special people who have achieved something in various careers.

Moreover, this kind of thinking is very suitable for the tastes of a part of the people who have already occupied a position on the screen. They think they are uniquely blessed by heaven. Heaven gave them to be stars, just like the former emperors received their mandate from heaven. They believe that you are ordinary people who are not blessed to receive the mandate of heaven, and you can only look up to their successful performance skills. Of course, you can forget about becoming a star in this life. The honors and rights of stars should be exclusively enjoyed and occupied by their genius forever.
